vatau dṛgādiṣu ca parataḥ sarvādīnām ākāro bhavati. yāvat, tāvat. yādṛk, tādṛk. yādṛśaḥ, tādṛśaḥ. yādṛkṣaḥ, tādṛkṣaḥ.

viṣvagdevayoś ca ḍadrig añci vau (5.2.109)
viṣvagdevayoḥ sarvādīnāṃ cāñcatau vipare parato ḍadrigāgamo bhavati. viṣvag añcati, viṣvadryaṅ. devadryaṅ, yadrayaṅ, tadryaṅ. vāv iti kim? viṣvagañcī.

samaḥ samiḥ (5.2.110)
samo 'ñcatau vipare samyādeśo bhavati. samyaṅ, samyañcau, samyañcaḥ; samīcaḥ, samīcā.

sahasya sadhrīḥ (5.2.111)
sahasyāñcatau vipare parataḥ sadhryādeśo bhavati. sadhryaṅ, sadhryañcau, sadhryañcaḥ; sadhrīcaḥ, sadhrīcā.

tirasas tiry ati (5.2.112)
tiraso 'ñcatāv akārādau paratas tiryādeśo bhavati. tiryaṅ, tiryañcau, tiryañcaḥ. atīti kim? tiraścaḥ, tiraścā.

dvyantaḥprāder anād apa īt (5.2.113)
dver antaḥśabdāt prādibhyaś cānavarṇāntebhyaḥ parasyāpa īdādeśo bhavati. dvīpaḥ, antarīpaḥ. samīpaḥ, nīpaḥ. anād iti kim? prāpam, parāpam.

deśe 'nūpaḥ (5.2.114)
deśe 'bhidheye 'nūpa iti nipātyate. anyatrānvīpaḥ.

samāpo nāmni (5.2.115)
Samāpa iti saṃjñāyāṃ nipātyate. Samāpaṃ nāma devayajanam. samīpam anyat.

chakārake 'nyasya duk (5.2.116)
che kārake ca parato 'nyasya dug āgamo bhavati. anyadīyaḥ, anyatkārakaḥ.

aṣaṣṭhītṛtīyasyāśīrāśāsthāsthitotsukotirāgeṣu (5.2.117)
aṣaṣṭhyantasyātṛtīyāntasya cānyasyāśīrādiṣu parato dug āgamo bhavati. anyā āśīḥ, anyadāśīḥ. anyadāśā, anyadāsthā, anyadāsthitaḥ, anyadutsukaḥ, anyadūtiḥ, anyadrāgaḥ. aṣaṣṭhītṛtīyasyeti kim? anyasyāśīḥ, anyāśīḥ. anyenāsthitaḥ, anyāsthitaḥ.

arthe vā (5.2.118)
arthe parato 'nyasya dug āgamo vā bhavati. anyadarthaḥ, anyārthaḥ. 

koḥ kad acy uttarārthe (5.2.119)
kuśabdasyottarapadārthe vartamānasyājādāv uttarapade kadādeśo bhavati. kaduṣṭraḥ, kadaśvaḥ. acīti kim? kubrāhmaṇaḥ. uttarārtha iti kim? kūṣṭro rājā.

trirathavadeṣu (5.2.120)
tryādiṣu parataḥ koḥ kadādeśo bhavati. kutsitās trayaḥ, kattrayaḥ. kadrathaḥ, kadvadaḥ.

tṛṇe jātau (5.2.121)
tṛṇe parato jātāv abhidheyāyāṃ koḥ kadādeśo bhavati. kattṛṇam. jātāv iti kim? kutsitāni tṛṇāni, kutṛṇāni.

kākṣapathoḥ (5.2.122)
akṣe pathi ca parataḥ koḥ kādeśo bhavati. kākṣaḥ, kāpathaḥ.

īṣadarthe (5.2.123)
īṣadarthe vartamānasya koḥ kādeśo bhavati. kāmadhuram, kālavaṇam, kāmlam.

puruṣe vā (5.2.124)
puruṣa uttarapade koḥ kābhāvo vā bhavati. kāpuruṣaḥ, kupuruṣaḥ. aprāptavibhāṣeyam. īṣadarthe tu pūrveṇa nityaṃ bhavati: īṣatpuruṣaḥ, kāpuruṣaḥ.

kavaṃ coṣṇe (5.2.125)
uṣṇe parataḥ koḥ kavaṃādeśo bhavati, kādeśaś ca vā. kavoṣṇam, koṣṇam, kaduṣṇam.

dikchabdāt tīrasya tāraḥ (5.2.126)
dikchabdāt parasya tīrasya tārādeśo vā bhavati. dakṣiṇatāram, dakṣiṇatīram. uttaratāram, uttaratīram.

pṛṣodarādīni (5.2.127)
pṛṣodarādīni śabdarūpāṇi sādhūni bhavanti. pṛṣad udaram asya, pṛṣodaraḥ - pṛṣad udvānam asya, pṛṣodvānaḥ - vārivāhako, balāhakaḥ - jīvanasya mūto, jīmūtaḥ - śavasya śayanam, śmaśānam - ūrdhvaṃ kham asya, udūkhalam, ulūkhalaṃ vā - piśitam aśnātīti piśācaḥ - bruvanto 'syāṃ sīdantīti bṛsī - mahyāṃ rautīti mayūraḥ - mahyāṃ śete, mahiṣaḥ - ṣaṭ ca daśa ca, ṣoḍaśa - kṛcchreṇa dāśyate, dūḍāśaḥ - kṛcchreṇa nāśyate, dūṇāśaḥ - kṛcchreṇa dabhyate, dūḍabhaḥ - duṣṭaṃ dhyāyatīti dūḍhyaḥ - Vāgvādasyāpatyam, Vāḍvaliḥ - divy oka eṣāṃ te divaukasaḥ. evam anye 'pi kapitthadadhitthāśvatthamahitthādayaḥ śiṣṭaprayogato 'nugantavyāḥ.
varṇāgamo varṇaviparyayaś ca,
dvau cāparau varṇavikāraṇāśau,
dhātos tadarthātiśayena yoga,
etac ca tat pañcavidhaṃ niruktam.

saṃkhyāvisāyāder ahnasyāhan ṅau vā (5.2.128)
saṃkhyāvisāyāder ahnaśabdasya ṅau parato ahanādeśo bhavati vā. dvayor ahnor bhave: dvyahni, dvyahani, dvyahne. vigate 'hani: vyahni, vyahani, vyahne. sāyāhni, sāyāhani, sāyāhne. saṃkhyāvisāyāder iti kim? pūrvāhṇe, aparāhṇe. ṅāv iti kim? dvyahnaḥ, vyahnaḥ, sāyāhnaḥ.

viśvasya vasurāṭor dairghaḥ (5.2.129)
vasurāṭor uttarapadayor viśvasya dīrgho bhavati. Viśvāvasuḥ, viśvārāṭ. rāḍ iti nirdeśād iha na bhavati: viśvarājau, viśvarājaḥ.

nare nāmni (5.2.130)
nare parataḥ saṃjñāyāṃ viśvasya dīrgho bhavati. Viśvānaraḥ. nāmnīti kim? viśvanaraḥ.

ṛṣau mitre (5.2.131)
ṛṣāv abhidheye mitre parato viśvasya dīrgho bhavati. Viśvāmitraḥ. ṛṣāv iti kim? Viśvamitro māṇavakaḥ. nāmnīty eva: viśvamitro muniḥ.

vanagiryoḥ koṭarāñjanādīnām (5.2.132)
vane girau ca parataḥ koṭarādīnām añjanādīnāṃ ca dīrgho bhavati. Koṭarāvaṇam - Miśrakāvaṇam - Sidhrakāvaṇam. Añjanāgiriḥ - Bhañjanāgiriḥ - Kiṃśukāgiriḥ. koṭarāñjanādīnām iti kim? Kuberavanam, Asipattravanam, Kṛṣṇagiriḥ. nāmnīty eva: añjanagiriḥ.

matau bahvaco 'najirādīnām (5.2.133)
matau parato bahvaco 'jirādivarjitasya dīrgho bhavati. Udumbarāvatī, Vīraṇāvatī. bahvaca iti kim? Vrīhimatī. anajirādīnām iti kim? Ajiravatī, Khadiravatī. nāmnīty eva: valayavatī. ajira - khadira - pulina - Malaya - kāraṇḍava - cakravāka.

śarādīnām (5.2.134)
śara ity evamādīnāṃ matau parato dīrgho bhavati. Śarāvatī, Vaṃśāvatī. nāmnīty eva: śaravatī. śara - vaṃśa - dhūma - ahi - kapi - maṇi - muni - śuci. ākṛtigaṇo 'yam.

vale (5.2.135)
vale parato dīrgho bhavati. kṛṣīvalaḥ, āsutīvalaḥ, dantāvalaḥ.

citeḥ kapi (5.2.136)
citiśabdasya kapi parato dīrgho bhavati. ekacitīkaḥ, dvicitīkaḥ.

ḍhralope 'ṇaḥ (5.2.137)
ḍhakārarephayor lopo yasmin tatra pūrvasyāṇo dīrgho bhavati. līḍham, gūḍham. nīraktam, dūraktam. aṇa iti kim? āvṛḍham.

sahivahor ot (5.2.138)
sahivahor ḍhralope 'ṇa ottvaṃ bhavati. soḍhā, voḍhā. soḍhum, voḍhum. udavoḍhām, udavoḍham. katham ūḍham? prād ūḍha (5.1.89) ityādiliṅgāt.

karṇe cihnasyāviṣṭāṣṭapañcabhinnacchinnacchidrasruvasvastikasya (5.2.139)
karṇe parataś cihnasya viṣṭādivarjitasya dīrgho bhavati. dātrākarṇaḥ, dviguṇākarṇaḥ, dvyaṅgulākarṇaḥ. cihnasyeti kim? śobhanakarṇaḥ. aviṣṭāder iti kim? viṣṭakarṇaḥ, aṣṭakarṇaḥ, pañcakarṇaḥ, bhinnakarṇaḥ, chinnakarṇaḥ, chidrakarṇaḥ, sruvakarṇaḥ, svastikakarṇaḥ.

nahivṛtivṛṣivyadhirucisahitaniṣu kvau (5.2.140)
nahyādiṣu kvibanteṣu parato dīrgho bhavati. upānat, nīvṛt, prāvṛt, marmāvit, nīruk, ṛṭīṣaṭ, parītat. gamādīnāṃ kvāv (5.3.49) ity anunāsikalopaḥ. kvāv iti kim? upanaddham.

prādīnāṃ ghañi bahulam (5.2.141)
prādīnāṃ ghañante parato bahulaṃ dīrgho bhavati. prativiśaty asmin niti pratīveśaḥ, prativeśaḥ. pratibodhanaṃ pratībodhaḥ. pratibodhaḥ. pratiharanti, jñāpayanty aneneti pratīhāraḥ, pratihāraḥ. pratikurvanti teneti pratīkāraḥ, pratikāraḥ. kvacid bhinaviṣaye: prakāraḥ, prākāraḥ; prasādaḥ, prāsādaḥ. kvacin na bhavati: Niṣādaḥ, viṣādaḥ. kvacid bhavaty eva: nīvāraḥ, nīhāraḥ, nīśāraḥ.

ikaḥ kāśe (5.2.142)
igantasya kāśe parato dīrgho bhavati. nīkāśaḥ, vīkāśaḥ, anūkāśaḥ, pratīkāśaḥ. ika iti kim? prakāśaḥ. bahulam ity eva: nikāśaḥ, vikāśaḥ. ajartha ārambhaḥ.

das ti (5.2.143)
dā ity asya yas takārādeśas tasmin parataḥ prādīnām igantānāṃ dīrgho bhavati. nīttam, parīttam, vīttam. tīti kim? sudattam. ika ity eva: prattam, avattam.

vahe (5.2.144)
vahe parata igantasya dīrgho bhavati. Ṛṣīvahaḥ, Kapīvahaḥ, Kṛṣīvahaḥ. ika ity eva: Piṇḍavahaḥ. bahulam ity eva: Pīluvahaḥ, Cāruvahaḥ.

anyeṣām api (5.2.145)
anyeṣām api śabdānām uttarapade bahulaṃ dīrgho bhavati. śvādantaḥ, śvādaṃṣṭraḥ, śvākarṇaḥ. kvacin na bhavati: Śvaphalkaḥ, śvamukhaḥ. kvacid viṣayāntare 'pi: śvapadam, śvāpadam. kvacid anuttarapade 'pi: puruṣaḥ, pūruṣaḥ.

cau (5.2.146)
añcatau luptākāre parato dīrgho bhavati. dadhīcaḥ, dadhīcā. madhūcaḥ, madhūcā.

yaṇa ikaḥ (5.2.147)
yaṇaḥ sthāne ya ik tasyottarapade dīrgho bhavati. Kārīṣagandhīputraḥ, Kaumudagandhīpatiḥ. yaṇa iti kim? bhūmipatiḥ.

pañcamasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ samāptaḥ.


prakṛteḥ (5.3.1)
ataḥ paraṃ prakṛter ity etad adhikṛtaṃ veditavyam.

halaḥ (5.3.2)
halaḥ prakṛtyavayavād uttaro yo yaṇa ik tadantāyāḥ prakṛter dīrgho bhavati. hūtaḥ, jīnaḥ, saṃvītaḥ. prakṛter ity eva: nirutam, durutam. tadantavidhiḥ kim? viddhaḥ, vicitaḥ. kathaṃ tṛtīyaḥ? dvitīyatṛtīyāv (4.2.59) iti nipātanāt.

aluki (5.3.3)
yatra yad ucyate tasyāluki sati tad bhavatīty etad adhikṛtaṃ veditavyam.

namy atisṛcatasroḥ (5.3.4)
nāmi paratas tisṛcatasṛvarjitāyāḥ prakṛter dīrgho bhavati. vṛkṣāṇām, agnīnām, vāyūnām, kartṝṇām. nuṭā nirdeśaḥ kim? kṛte nuṭi dīrghatvaprasiddhyartham. anyathā hi nuḍabhāvaḥ syāt. atisṛcatasror iti kim? tisṛṇām, catasṛṇām. alukīty eva: tālavanam, pīluvanam. prakṛter ity eva: kṛmiṇāṃ paśya, pāmanāṃ paśya. naiṣā nāmi prakṛtiḥ.

nur vā (5.3.5)
nṛśabdasya nāmi parato dīrgho vā bhavati. nṝṇām, nṛṇām.

naḥ (5.3.6)
nakārāntāyāḥ prakṛter nāmi parato dīrgho bhavati. pañcānām, saptānām. nāmīty eva: carmaṇām.

śisuṭi (5.3.7)
śau suṭi ca parato nakārāntāyāḥ prakṛter dīrgho bhavati. sāmāni, vemāni. kuṇḍāni, vanāni. numāpīha nāntatvaṃ sukhādīni (1.1.35) iti liṅgāt. rājānau, rājānaḥ, rājānam, rājānau. dīrghapratiyogino hrasvasya bhavati, vacanasāmarthyāc ca vyavadhānam āśrīyate. alukīty eva: rājaprāptaḥ.

smahator numi (5.3.8)
sakārāntasya mahataś ca śau suṭi ca parato numi sati pūrvasya dīrgho bahvati. śreyāṃsi, mahānti. śreyāṃsau, mahāntau. numīti kim? apsarasaḥ.

aptṛsvasṛnaptṛneṣṭṛtvaṣṭṛkṣattṛhotṛpotṛpraśāstṝṇām (5.3.9)
apśabdasya tṛjantasya tṛnantasya ca svasrādīnāṃ ca śau suṭi ca parato dīrgho bhavati. āpaḥ; kartṝṇi; kartāraṃ kaṭān, vaktāraṃ janāpavādān; svasāram, naptāram, neṣṭāram, tvaṣṭāram, kṣattāram, hotāram, potāram, praśāstāram. naptrādigrahaṇād anyeṣāṃ trantānāṃ saṃjñāábdānāṃ na bhavati: mātaram, pitaram, jāmātaram, duhitaram, bhrātaram.

sāv asaṃbuddhau (5.3.10)
sau yad dīrghatvaṃ tad asaṃbodhana eva bhavati. rājā; śreyān, mahān; kartā, svasā, naptā, neṣṭā, tvaṣṭā, kṣattā, hotā, potā, praśāstā. saṃbuddhau na bhavati: he rājan, he śreyan, he mahan, he kartaḥ.

atvasoḥ (5.3.11)
atvantasyāsantasya ca sāv asaṃbuddhau dīrgho bhavati. bhavān, kṛtavān, gomān. matupaḥ pakārānubandho, na punar atuśabdasya, ity asyāpi bhavati. asantasya ca: apsarāḥ, sumanāḥ. katham: carma vaste, carmava iti? atusāhacaryād adhātor eva grahaṇam. asaṃbuddhāv ity eva: he bhavan, he sumanaḥ.

inhanapūṣāryamṇāṃ śau ca (5.3.12)
inantasya hanādīnāṃ ca śāv eva dīrgho bhavati, sau cāsaṃbuddhau. daṇḍīni, daṇḍī. bhrūṇahāni, bhrūṇahā. bahupūṣāṇi, Pūṣā bahvaryamāṇi, Aryamā. sau ceti kim? daṇḍinau, daṇḍinaḥ; Vṛtrahaṇam, Pūṣaṇam, Aryamaṇam. asaṃbuddhāv ity eva: he daṇḍin, he Vṛtrahan, he Pūṣan, he Aryaman. asmād eva niyamād uttaram api na dīrghatvam: bhrūṇahani. upāntadīrghaniyamāt: vṛtrahāyate.

ajjhanoḥ sani jhali (5.3.13)
ajantasya hanteś ca sani jhalādau parato dīrgho bhavati. cikīrṣati, tuṣṭūṣati, cicīṣati; jighāṃsati. jhalīti kim? yiyaviṣati. prakṛter ity eva: dadhi sanoti.

iṅo gamaḥ (5.3.14)
iṅādeśasya gamaḥ sani jhalādau parato dīrgho bhavati. adhijigāṃsate vedam. iṅa iti kim? saṃjigaṃsate.

tano vā (5.3.15)
tanoteḥ sani jhalādau parato dīrgho vā bhavati. titāṃsati, titaṃsati. jhalīty eva: titaniṣati.

kramas tvi (5.3.16)
kramas tvi parato dīrgho vā bhavati. krāntvā, krantvā. jhalīty eva: kramitvā, prakramya.

ñamaḥ kiti vau ca (5.3.17)
ñamantasya vau kiti jhalādau ca parato dīrgho vā bhavati. praśān, pratān. śāntaḥ, śāntavān. ñama iti kim? odanapak. kitīti kim? gantā. vau ceti kim? gamyate.

ñami ca cchavoḥ śūṭh (5.3.18) 
ñami parato vau jhalādau ca satukaḥ chakārasya śakārādeśo bhavati, vakārasya ca ūṭh. viśnaḥ, praśnaḥ; prāṭ; pṛṣṭaḥ, praṣṭā, praṣṭum. syonam; akṣadyūḥ; dudyūṣati, dyūtvā, dyūtam. kathaṃ dyubhyāṃ, dyubhir iti? ūṭhi kṛte diva ud (5.1.135 bez. P. 6.1.131) iti taparatvān mātrākālo bhaviṣyati. ñami ceti kim? devitvā. kathaṃ pratidīvnā? bahiraṅgasyāllopasyāsiddhatvān na bhaviṣyati.

jvaratvarāvaśrivumavāṃ sopāntasya (5.3.19)
jvarādīnāṃ vakārasyopāntasahitasya vau jhalādau ca parata ūṭh bhavati. jūḥ, jūrau, jūrtiḥ. tūḥ, tūrau, tūrtiḥ, tūrṇavān. ūḥ, uvau, ūtiḥ. śrūḥ, śruvau, śrūtiḥ. mūḥ, muvau, mūtiḥ. 

rāl lopaḥ (5.3.20)
rephāt parayoś chvor vau jhalādau ca parato lopo bhavati. murchā: mūḥ, murau, mūrtiḥ. dhurvī: dhūḥ, dhurau, dhūrtiḥ. vau cety eva: mūrchā.

prāg yuvor avugyug asiddhaṃ samānāśraye (5.3.21)
prāg yuvusaṃśabdanād (5.4.1) vukā yukā ca varjitaṃ kāryaṃ samānāśraye kāryāntare kartavye 'siddhaṃ veditavyam. edhi, śādhi: ettvaśātvayor asiddhatvāj jhallakṣaṇaṃ dhitvaṃ bhavati. jahi: jatvasyāsiddhatvād dher lug na bhavati. tatra tasya ca bhāvāt samānāśrayatvam eteṣām. samānāśrayalakṣaṇaś cātra vidhir, na vyāśrayalakṣaṇaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ. prāg yuvor iti kim? abhāji, rāgaḥ. ākāre kartavye nalopaḥ siddha eva. avugyug iti kim? babhūvatuḥ, upadidīye. vugyukoḥ siddhatvād uvyaṇādeśau na bhavataḥ. samānāśraya iti kim? papuṣaḥ, cicyuṣaḥ, luluvuṣaḥ. vasor ud vibhaktyāśrayeṣu ālopayaṇuvādeśeṣu kartavyeṣu nāsiddhaḥ. asmād eva vacanād bahiraṅgaparibhāṣā nehāśrīyate, bahiraṅgasya cāntaraṅganimittatvāt.

śnān naḥ (5.3.22)
śnamaḥ parasya nakārasya lopo bhavati. bhanakti, vyanakti. śakāraḥ kim? prayatnānām. praśnānām iti lākṣaṇikatvād anarthakatvāc ca na bhavati.

halo 'niditaḥ kṅity upāntasya (5.3.23)
halantāyāḥ prakṛter aniditaḥ kṅiti parata upāntanakārasya lopo bhavati. srastaḥ, srasyate. dhvastaḥ, dhvasyate. sanīsrasyate, danīdhvasyate. hala iti kim? nīyate. anidita iti kim? nandyate. kṅitīti kim? sraṃsitā. upāntasyeti kim? nahyate.

śity apiti (5.3.24)
śity apiti parato 'nidita upāntanakārasya lopo bhavati. dabhnoti, mathnāti, śrathnāti, grathnāti. apitīti kim? sraṃsate, dhvaṃsate. anidita ity eva: śiñjānaḥ.

liṭīndhiśranthagranthām (5.3.25)
liṭi parata indhādīnāṃ nalopo bhavati. samīdhe; śrethatuḥ, śrethuḥ; grethatuḥ, grethuḥ. eṣām iti kim? sasraṃse. apitīty eva: śaśrantha.

dambhaḥ ssani ca (5.3.26)
dambheḥ sakārādau sani liṭi cāpiti parato nalopo bhavati. dhipsati, debhatuḥ, debhuḥ. dvisakāranirdeśaḥ kim? didhambiṣati.

svañjaḥ (5.3.27)
svañjer liṭi parato nalopo bhavati. pariṣasvaje. sadisvañjer liṭi (6.4.98) iti ṣatvapratiṣedhaḥ.

śapi daṃśasañjeś ca (5.3.28)
śapi parato daṃśeḥ sañjeḥ svañjaś ca nalopo bhavati. daśati, sajati, pariṣvajate.

rañjaḥ (5.3.29)
rañjaḥ śapi parato nalopo bhavati. rajati. kathaṃ rajanam, rajatam. raja iti? auṇādikā ete. tathā hi: rajaḥ kyun, pṛṣirañjibhyāṃ kid ity atac, uṣirañjibhyāṃ kid ity asun.

ṇau mṛgaramaṇe (5.3.30)
ṇau parato mṛgaramaṇe gamyamāne rañjer nalopo bhavati. rajayati mṛgān. atra mittvād dhrasvatvam. mṛgaramaṇa iti kim? rañjayati vastrāṇi. kathaṃ rāgī? ininā siddham.

ghañi bhāvakaraṇayoḥ (5.3.31)
bhāvakaraṇayor yo ghañ tasmin parato rañjer nalopo bhavati. rañjanam, rajaty aneneti rāgaḥ. bhāvakaraṇayor iti kim? rajanti tasmin niti raṅgaḥ.

syado jave (5.3.32)
syada iti syander ghañi nipātyate, jave 'bhidheye. anyatra tailasyandaḥ.

avodaidhaudmapraśrathahimaśrathaḥ (5.3.33)
avoda ity under ghañi nipātyate, edha iti indheḥ, odma iti under manini, praśrathaḥ śrantheḥ prapūrvasya ghañi, himaśratha iti himapūrvasya.

laṅgikampyor upatāpaśarīra vikārayoḥ (5.3.34)
laṅgeḥ kampeś copatāpe śarīravikāre cārthe nalopo bhavati. vilagitaḥ, vikapitaḥ. anyatra vilaṅgitaḥ, vikamppitaḥ. vṛṃher acy aniṭīti na vācyam. nivarhati, nivarhaka iti vṛhiṇā siddham; halādāv iṭi ca dṛśyate: nivṛhyate, nivarhitā. vṛṃhes tu nivṛṃhati, nivṛṃhakaḥ, nivṛṃhyate, nivṛṃhitā.

tanādyaniṭvanāṃ lyapi ñamaḥ (5.3.35)
tanādīnām aniṭāṃ vanaś ca lyapi parato ñamo lopo bhavati. pratatya, prakṛtya; prahatya, pramatya; pravatya. eṣām iti kim? praśasya. lyapīti kim? yamyate, ramyate.

mo vā (5.3.36)
tanādyaniṭvanāṃ lyapi parato makārasya lopo vā bhavati. prayatya, prayamya. viratya, viramya. praṇatya, praṇamya. āgatya, āgamya.

jhali tiṅy apiti (5.3.37)
tiṅy apiti jhalādau paratas tanādyaniṭvanāṃ ñamo lopo bhavati. hataḥ, hathaḥ. jhalīti kim? ghnanti. tiṅīti kim? hantā. apitīti kim? hanti.

kṅiti (5.3.38)
kiti ṅiti jhalādau paratas tanādyaniṭvanāṃ ñamo lopo bhavati. tataḥ, tatavān. kṣataḥ, kṣatavān. yataḥ, yatavān. rataḥ, ratavān. vatiḥ ktini; ktici pratiṣedhaṃ vakṣyati (5.3.43), anyatra ceṭā bhavitavyam. jhalīty eva: hanyate, gamyate. tanādyaniṭvanām ity eva: śāntaḥ, śāntavān. dāntaḥ, dāntavān. ñama ity eva: pakvaḥ.

janasanakhanām āt (5.3.39)
janādīnāṃ jhali kṅiti parato ñama ād bhavati. jātaḥ, jātavān. sātaḥ, sātavān. khātaḥ, khātavān. kṅitīty eva: jantuḥ. jhalīty eva: janitvā.

sani (5.3.40)
janādīnāṃ sani jhalādau parato ñama ād bhavati. siṣāsati. janakhanor iṭā bhavitavyam. jhalīty eva: sisaniṣati.

ye vā (5.3.41)
ye kṅiti parato janādīnām āttvaṃ vā bhavati. jāyate, janyate; jājāyate, jañjanyate. sāyate, sanyate; sāsāyate, saṃsanyate. khāyate, khanyate; cākhāyate, caṅkhanyate.

tano yaki (5.3.42)
tanoter yaki parata āttvaṃ vā bhavati. tāyate, tanyate.

sanaḥ ktici lopaś ca (5.3.43)
sanaḥ ktici parato lopa āttvaṃ ca vā bhavati. satiḥ, sātiḥ, santiḥ.

liṅi taṅi gamaḥ (5.3.44)
liṅi taṅbhūte parato gamer lopo vā bhavati. saṃgasīṣṭa. saṃgaṃsīṣṭa. liṅīti kim? saṃjagme. taṅīti kim? gamyāt. 

sici (5.3.45)
sici taṅpare parato gamer lopo vā bhavati. samagata, samagaṃsta.

hanaḥ (5.3.46)
hanteḥ sici parato lopo bhavati, nityaṃ yogavibhāgāt. āhata, āhasātām.

yamaḥ sūcane (5.3.47)
yameḥ sūcane vartamānasya sici taṅpare parato lopo bhavati. udāyata, udāyasātām. sūcana iti kim? āyaṃsta pādam. jhali tiṅy apity api na bhavati, sicā vyavadhānāt. taṅīty eva: ayaṃsīt.

vodvāhe (5.3.48)
udvāhe vartamānasya yameḥ sici taṅpare parato lopo vā bhavati. upāyata kanyām, upāyaṃsta kanyām.

gamādīnāṃ kvau (5.3.49)
gamādīnāṃ kvau parato lopo bhavati. janagat, saṃyat, parītat. katham agregūḥ? auṇādiko ḍūr bhaviṣyati.

nāñcaḥ pūjāyām (5.3.50)
añcateḥ pūjāyāṃ gamyamānāyāṃ nalopo na bhavati. añcitam iva śiro vahati. pūjāyām iti kim? udaktam udakaṃ kūpāt.

ktici dīrghaś ca (5.3.51)
ktici parato nalopo dīrghaś ca na bhavati. tantiḥ, rantiḥ, vantiḥ. kticaḥ saṃjñāyāṃ vacanāt sañjādīnām aprayogaḥ. kathaṃ saktir, bhaktir iti? ktinā siddham. dīrghasaṃbhave vā lopapratiṣedhaḥ.

ktvi skandasyandoḥ (5.3.52)
ktvi parataḥ skandaḥ syandeś ca nalopo na bhavati. skantvā, syantvā.

seṭi (5.3.53)
seṭi ktvi parato parato nalopo na bhavati. sraṃsitvā, dhvaṃsitvā, syanditvā.

vañciluñcithapho vā (5.3.54)
vañciluñces thāntānāṃ phāntānāṃ ca seṭi parato nalopo vā na bhavati. vañcitvā, vacitvā. luñcitvā, lucitvā. śranthitvā, śrathitvā. granthitvā, grathitvā. gumphitvā, guphitvā.

janaśaḥ (5.3.55)
jāntānāṃ naśeś ca ktvi parato nalopo vā bhavati. bhaṅktvā, bhaktvā. naṃṣṭvā, naṣṭvā. yogavibhāgo 'niḍarthaḥ.

bhañjeś ciṇi (5.3.56)
bhañjeś ciṇi parato nalopo vā bhavati. abhāji, abhañji.

śāsaḥ kṅiti śis (5.3.57)
śāsaḥ kṅiti parataḥ śisādeśo bhavati. śiṣṭaḥ, anvaśiṣat, śeśiṣyate, mitraśīḥ, āśīḥ. kṅitīti kim? śāstā.

tiṅi haly apiti (5.3.58)
tiṅi halādāv apiti parataḥ śāsaḥ śisādeśo bhavati. tau śiṣṭaḥ, vayaṃ śiṣmaḥ. tiṅīti kim? śāstram. halīti kim? śaśāsatuḥ. apitīti kim? śāsti.

śā hau (5.3.59)
śāso hau parataḥ śādeśo bhavati. śādhi.

hano jaḥ (5.3.60)
hanter hau parato jādeśo bhavati. jahi.

liḍāśīrliṅatiṅśiti (5.3.61)
liṭy āśīrliṅy atiṅśiti caitad adhikṛtaṃ veditavyam.

bhrasjo bharj vā (5.3.62)
bhrasjer liḍādiṣu bharjādeśo vā bhavati. babharja, babhrajja. bharkṣīṣṭa, bhrakṣīṣṭa. bharṣṭā, bhraṣṭā. kathaṃ bhṛjjyāt, bhṛṣṭaḥ, barībhṛjjyata iti? vyavasthitavibhāṣayā, bhrasja iti rūpāśrayaṇād vā. pūrvaṃ ca yaṇa ik pūrvavipratiṣedhāt.

lopo 'taḥ (5.3.63)
adantāyāḥ prakṛter liḍādiṣu parato lopo bhavati. cikīrṣāṃcakāra, lolūyāṃcakre. cikīrṣyāt. cikīrṣitā. lopavidher balavattvād ākāro na bhavati. cikīrṣakaḥ, cikīrṣyate. liḍādiṣv ity eva: cikīrṣati.

yaki (5.3.64)
yaki parataḥ prakṛter ato lopo bhavati. kusubhyati, magadhyati. kakāraḥ kim? śyenāyate.

yasya halaḥ (5.3.65)
halaḥ parasya yasya liḍādiṣu lopo bhavati. bebhidāṃcakre, bebhidiṣīṣṭa, bebhiditā. akāraḥ kim? īrṣyitā, madhyitā. hala iti kim? lolūyitā. athavā halantāyāḥ prakṛter vihitasya lopo bhavati. halantāyā iti kim? īrṣyitā, madhyitā. kaḥ punar anayoḥ sūtrārthayor viśeṣaḥ? yadā pūrvas tadā sosūtritā, śāśayiteti bhavitavyam. yadāparas tadā sosūtryitā, śāśayyiteti bhavitavyam. liḍādiṣv ity eva: bebhidyate.

kyasya vā (5.3.66)
halaḥ parasya kyasya liḍādiṣu lopo vā bhavati. samidhāṃcakāra, samidhyāṃcakāra. dṛṣadāṃcakre, dṛṣadyāṃcakre. samidhiṣīṣṭa, samidhyiṣīṣṭa. samidhitā, samidhyitā. hala ity eva: paṭīyitā, paṭāyitā. kecid yako 'pi vā lopam icchanti: bhiṣajyitā, bhiṣajitā. tad anarthakam, kyacā kyaṅā vā siddhatvāt.

ṇer aniṭi (5.3.67)
aniṭi liḍādau parato ṇer lopo bhavati. iyyaṇadeṅādaijdīrghāṇām apavādaḥ. atatakṣat, āṭīṭat, kāraṇā, kārakaḥ, kāryate. aniṭīti kim? kārayitā. liḍādiṣv ity eva: kārayati.

tatavatīṭi (5.3.68)
ktaktavatvor iḍādyoḥ parato ṇer lopo bhavati. iyyaṇadeṅādaijdīrghāṇām apavādaḥ. atatakṣat, āṭiṭat, kāraṇā, kārakaḥ, kāryate. aniṭīti kim? kārayitā. liḍādiṣv ity eva: kārayati.

ay āmantālvāyyetnuṣu (5.3.69)
ktaktavatvor iḍādyoḥ parato ṇer lopo bhavati. kāritam, kāritavān. hāritam, hāritavān. iṭīti kim? iṭi kṛte ṇilopo yathā syāt. anyathā hi lope kṛte ekāca (5.4.130) iti iḍ na bhavati. saṃjñapitaḥ paśuḥ. iḍgrahaṇasāmarthyāt pūrveṇāpi na bhavati. sanīvantardha (5.4.119) ityādinā vikalpita iṭ, yato 'pater vā (5.4.140) iti pratiṣedhaḥ.

lyapi laghoḥ (5.3.70)
lyapi parato laghoḥ parasya ṇer ayādeśo bhavati. praśamayya gataḥ, prabebhidayya gataḥ, pragaṇayya gataḥ. vacanasāmarthyād vyavadhānam āśrīyate. yalopāllopayor vyāśrayatvād asiddhatvaṃ nāsti. ṇau yalopāllopau, lyapi ṇer ayādeśaḥ. laghor iti kim? pratipādya gataḥ.

āpo vā (5.3.71)
āpaḥ parasya ṇer lyapi parato 'yādeśo vā bhavati. prāpayya gataḥ, prāpya gataḥ. adhyāpyeti lākṣaṇikatvān na bhavati.

kṣeḥ kṣīḥ (5.3.72)
kṣer lyapi parataḥ kṣībhāvo bhavati. prakṣīya, upakṣīya.

upadeśe'jjhanagrahadṛgbhyaḥ syasicsīyuṭtāsāṃ bhāvāpyayoś ciṇvad iṭ vā (5.3.73)
upadeśe 'jantebhyo hanādibhyaś ca pareṣāṃ syādīnāṃ bhāvāpyaviṣaye ciṇvad iḍāgamo vā bhavati. cāyiṣyate, ceṣyate; dāyiṣyate, dāsyate; śamiṣyate, śāmiṣyate, śamayiṣyate; ghāniṣyate, haniṣyate; grāhiṣyate, grahīṣyate; darśiṣyate, drakṣyate. acāyiṣātām, aceṣātām; adāyiṣātām, adiṣātām; aśamiṣātām, aśāmiṣātām, aśamayiṣātām; aghāniṣātām, avadhiṣātām; agrāhiṣātām, agrahīṣātām; adarśiṣātām, adṛkṣātām. cāyiṣīṣṭa, ceṣīṣṭa; dāyiṣīṣṭa, dāsīṣṭa; śamiṣīṣṭa, śāmiṣīṣṭa, śamayiṣīṣṭa; ghāniṣīṣṭa, vadhiṣīṣṭa; grāhiṣīṣṭa, grahīṣīṣṭa; darśiṣīṣṭa, dṛkṣīṣṭa. cāyitā, cetā; dāyitā, dātā; śamitā, śāmitā, śamayitā; ghānitā, hantā; grāhitā, grahītā; darśitā, draṣṭā. upadeśa iti kim? kāriṣyate. ajjhanagrahadṛgbhya iti kim? paṭhiṣyate. syasicsīyuṭtāsām iti kim? cetavyam. bhāvāpyayor iti kim? ceṣyati. ciṇvadbhāvāc ciṇāśrayaṃ kāryaṃ bhavati, luṅāśrayaṃ na bhavati. ato haniṇiṅām ādeśā na bhavanti: aghāniṣātām, āyiṣātām, adhyāyiṣātām.

dīṅo liṭi yuk (5.3.74)
dīṅo liṭi parato yugāgamo bhavati. upadidīye, upadidīyāte. liṭīti kim? upadedīyate.

lopo 'ci kṅiti cātaḥ (5.3.75)
ajādau liṭi kṅiti ca parata ādantāyāḥ prakṛter lopo bhavati. godaḥ, kambaladaḥ. saṃsthā, avasthā. yayau, yayatuḥ, yayuḥ. yayitha. acīti kim? dīyate. kṅitīti kim? dānam.

īd yati (5.3.76)
yati parata āta īdādeśo bhavati. gleyam, mleyam, deyam, dheyam, heyam.

māsthāsāgāpibahāgdādhāṁ hali (5.3.77)
mādīnāṃ hali kṅiti parata īd bhavati. mīyate, memīyate. sthīyate, teṣṭhīyate. avasīyate, avaseṣīyate. gīyate, jegīyate. pīyate, pepīyate. hīyate, jehīyate. dīyate, dedīyate. dhīyate, dedhīyate. pibeti kim? pāyate. kakāraḥ kim? hāyate. halīti kim? godaḥ. kṅitīty eva: dātā.

liṅy et (5.3.78)
liṅi parato mādīnām ed bhavati. meyāt, stheyāt, avaseyāt, geyāt, peyāt, heyāt, deyāt, dheyāt. kṅitīty eva: dāsīṣṭa.

vā saṃyogāder asthaḥ (5.3.79)
saṃyogāder ākārāntāyāḥ prakṛteḥ sthāvarjitāyā liṅy ed vā bhavati. gleyāt, glāyāt. mleyāt, mlāyāt. saṃyogāder iti kim? yāyāt. astha iti kim? stheyāt. kṅitīty eva: glāsīṣṭa. āśīrliṅīty eva: mlāyet. prakṛter ity eva: niryāyāt.

na lyapi (5.3.80)
lyapi parato mādīnāṃ yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati. pramāya, prasthāya, avasāya, pragāya, prapāya, prahāya, pradāya, pradhāya.

meṅa id vā (5.3.81)
meṅo lyapi parata idādeśo vā bhavati. apamitya, apamāya.

luṅlaṅlṛṅkṣv aḍ amāṅyoge (5.3.82)
luṅādiṣu parataḥ prakṛter aḍāgamo bhavati, na cen māṅyogo bhavati. akārṣīt, akarot, akariṣyat. amāṅyoga iti kim? mā bhavān kārṣīt; mā sma karot. prakṛter ity eva: prākarot.

aci śnudhātubhruvāṃ yvor iyuvau (5.3.83)
aci parata ivarṇovarṇayor iyuvau bhavataḥ, tau cec śnudhātubhrūsaṃbandhino bhavataḥ. āpnuvanti; cikṣiyatuḥ, cikṣiyuḥ; luluvatuḥ, luluvuḥ; śriyau, śriyaḥ; bhruvau, bhruvaḥ. acīti kim? prāpnuyāt. śnudhātubhruvām iti kim? lakṣmyau, lakṣmyaḥ. yvor iti kim? cakratuḥ, cakruḥ. prakṛter iti eva: śryarthaḥ.

dvitve pūrvasyāsame (5.3.84)
dvirvacane sati pūrvasyātulye 'ci ivarṇovarṇayor iyuvau bhavataḥ. iyeṣa, uvoṣa, iyarti. asama iti kim? ījatuḥ, ījuḥ. ūṣatuḥ, ūṣuḥ. acīty eva: iyāja, uvāca.

striyāḥ (5.3.85)
striyā ivarṇasyāci parata iyādeśo bhavati. striyau, striyaḥ. acīty eva: strībhiḥ.

vāmśasoḥ (5.3.86)
striyā ivarṇasyāmi śasi ca parata iyādeśo vā bhavati. striyam, strīm. striyaḥ, strīḥ.

iṇo yaṇ (5.3.87)
iṇaḥ prakṛter aci parato yaṇādeśo bhavati. yanti, yantu. iyo 'pavādaḥ.

er asaṃyogād anekācaḥ (5.3.88)
asaṃyogāt paro ya ivarṇas tadantāyāḥ prakṛter anekāco 'ci parato yaṇādeśo bhavati. ninyatuḥ, ninyuḥ. er iti kim? luluvatuḥ, luluvuḥ. asaṃyogād iti kim? cikriyatuḥ, cikriyuḥ. anekāca iti kim? adhīyāte.

kārakāsaṃkhyād oś ca supy asudhiyaḥ (5.3.89)
kārakād asaṃkhyāc ca parasyāḥ prakṛter ivarṇāntāyā uvarṇāntāyāś ca sudhīvarjitāyāḥ supy ajādau parato yaṇ bhavati, na cet saṃyogāt parāv ivarṇovarṇau bhavataḥ. grāmaṇyau, grāmaṇyaḥ; unnyau, unnyaḥ. khalapvau, khalapvaḥ; sakṛllvau, sakṛllvaḥ. kārakāsaṃkhyād iti kim? paramaniyau, paramaniyaḥ. paramaluvau, paramaluvaḥ. niyau, niyaḥ. luvau, luvaḥ. supīty kim? upaluluvuḥ. asudhiya iti kim? sudhiyau, sudhiyaḥ. asaṃyogād ity eva: yavakriyau, yavakriyaḥ. kaṭapruvau, kaṭapruvaḥ.

varṣādṛnpunaḥkārād bhuvaḥ (5.3.90)
varṣādibhya eva parasya bhuvaḥ supy ajādau parato yaṇ bhavati. varṣābhvau, varṣābhvaḥ. dṛnbhvau, dṛnbhvaḥ. punarbhvau, punarbhvaḥ. kārabhvau, kārabhvaḥ. varṣādibhya iti kim? ātmabhuvau, ātmabhuvaḥ. pratibhuvau, pratibhuvaḥ.

huśnuvor aliṭi (5.3.91)
hu śnu ity etayor liḍvarjite 'jādau parato yaṇ bhavati. juhvati, juhvatu, juhvat. sunvanti, cinvanti. huśnuvor iti kim? yuvanti, ruvanti. aliṭīti kim? juhuvatuḥ, juhuvuḥ. asaṃyogād ity eva: āpnuvanti, rādhnuvanti.

bhuvo vug luṅliṭoḥ (5.3.92)
bhavater luṅi liṭi cājādau parato vug āgamo bhavati. abhūvan. babhūva, babhūvatuḥ, babhūvuḥ.

ūd goho 'caḥ (5.3.93)
goher ajādau parato 'ca ūdādeśo bhavati. nigūhayati, nigūhakaḥ. okāranirdeśaḥ kim? nijuguhatuḥ, nijuguhuḥ. aca iti kim? antyasya mā bhūt. acīty eva: nigoḍhā.

duṣo ṇau (5.3.94)
duṣo ṇau parato 'ca ūdādeśo bhavati. dūṣayati. ṇāv iti kim? doṣaḥ.

vā citte (5.3.95)
cittaviṣayasya duṣo ṇāv aca ūdādeśo vā bhavati. dūṣayati cittam, doṣayati cittam. cittagrahaṇenaiva caitasikasyāpi grahaṇāt prajñāṃ doṣayati, prajñāṃ dūṣayati.

gamajanakhanaghasāṃ le lopo 'piti (5.3.96)
gamādīnāṃ lādeśe 'jādāv apiti parato 'co lopo bhavati. jagmatuḥ, jagmuḥ, jagmivān. jajñatuḥ, jajñuḥ, jajñe, jajñāte, jajñire. cakhnatuḥ, cakhnuḥ. jakṣatuḥ, jakṣuḥ, jakṣivān. la iti kim? agamat. apitīti kim? jagāma.

kiti ca hanaḥ (5.3.97)
kiti lādeśe 'piti cājādau parato hanter aco lopo bhavati. jāyāghnaḥ, nighnaḥ, vighnaḥ; jaghnatuḥ, jaghnuḥ, jaghnivān. acīty eva: hataḥ, hathaḥ.

hujhalo 'niṭo her dhiḥ (5.3.98)
juhoter jhalantāyāś ca prakṛteḥ parasyāniṭo her dhibhāvo bhavati. juhudhi, bhinddhi, chinddhi. hujhala iti kim? krīṇīhi. aniṭa iti kim? rudihi, svapihi. her iti kim? juhotu. juhutāt, bhinttād ity antaraṅgatvāt tātaṅ. tasya punar na dhibhāvo her iti rūpāśrayaṇāt.

ato luk (5.3.99)
ataḥ parasya her lug bhavati. paca, paṭha. ata iti kim? ehi. taparaḥ kim? yāhi.

uto 'saṃyogād adhātoḥ (5.3.100)
asaṃyogāt paro ya ukāras tasmād adhātoḥ parasya her lug bhavati. kuru, cinu. uta iti kim? lunīhi, punīhi. asaṃyogād iti kim? āpnuhi, śaknuhi. adhātor iti kim? yuhi, ruhi.

vāsya vmoḥ (5.3.101)
vakāramakārayoḥ parato 'syety uto 'saṃyogād adhātoḥ parasya lug vā bhavati. tanvaḥ, tanuvaḥ; tanmaḥ, tanumaḥ. sunvaḥ, sunuvaḥ; sunmaḥ, sunumaḥ. asaṃyogād ity eva: śaknuvaḥ, śaknumaḥ. adhātor ity eva: yuvaḥ, yumaḥ.

kṛño ye ca (5.3.102)
karoteḥ parasyoto ye vmoś ca parato lug bhavati. kuryāt, kuryātām. kurvaḥ, kurmaḥ.

ata ut tatrāpiti (5.3.103)
karoter uti parato 'ta ud bhavati, pitpare tu na bhavati. kurugaḥ, kurvanti, kurvan. ud iti taparatvam adeṅnivṛttyartham. tatreti kim? kartā. apitīti kim? karoti, karoṣi. ye cety eva: kuryāt. kurvaḥ, kurma ity ukāralopasyāsiddhatvād uttvaṃ bhavati.

śnasor lopaḥ (5.3.104)
śnamo 'steś cāpiti parato 'to lopo bhavati. runddhaḥ, rundhanti. staḥ, santi. apitīty eva: ruṇaddhi, asti.

śnādviruktayor ātaḥ (5.3.105)
śno dviruktāyāś ca prakṛter ākārasyāpiti parato lopo bhavati. lunate, lunatām; punate, punatām. mimate, mimatām; saṃjihate, saṃjihatām. śnādviruktayor iti kim? yānti, vānti. āta iti kim? bibhrati. apitīty eva: alunām, ajahām.

ī hali tiṅy adādhaḥ (5.3.106)
śno dviruktāyāś ca prakṛter dādhāvarjitāyā ākārasya halādāv apiti parata īd bhavati. lunītaḥ, punītaḥ. mimīte, saṃjihīte. halīti kim? lunanti, punanti; mimate. tiṅīti kim? saṃjihāsate. adādha iti kim? dattaḥ, dhattaḥ. apitīty eva: lunāti, jahāti.

id daridraḥ (5.3.107)
daridrāter halādau tiṅy apiti parata ikāro bhavati. daridritaḥ, daridrithaḥ. halīty eva: daridrati. tiṅīty eva: didaridrāsati. apitīty eva: daridrāti.

bhiyo vā (5.3.108)
bibheter hali tiṅy apiti parata ikāro vā bhavati. bibhitaḥ, bibhītaḥ. bibhithaḥ, bibhīthaḥ. halīty eva: bibhyati. tiṅīty eva: bibhīṣati, bhītaḥ. apitīty ava: bibheti.

hākaḥ (5.3.109)
jahāter hali tiṅy apiti parata ikāro vā bhavati. jahitaḥ, jahītaḥ. jahithaḥ, jahīthaḥ. halīty eva: jahati. tiṅīty eva: jihāsati. apitīty eva: jahāti.

hau vā (5.3.110)
jahāter hau parata ittvam ītvaṃ ca vā bhavati. jahihi, jahīhi, jahāhi.

yi lopaḥ (5.3.111)
yakārādau tiṅi parato jahāter lopo bhavati. jahyāt, jahyātām. tiṅīty eva: hīyate. kathaṃ heyāt? liṅy ed (5.3.78) ity anavakāśatvāt.

daridraḥ kiti (5.3.112)
daridrāter yakārādau kiti parato lopo bhavati. daridryate, daridryāt. kitīti kim? daridrāyāt.

acy ayuvau (5.3.113)
ajādau yuvuvarjite parato daridrāter lopo bhavati. daridrati, adaridran; daridritā, daridritum; didaridriṣati; daridraḥ. āto ṇe 'pi yug na bhavati, lopavidher balavattvāt. acīti kim? didaridrāsati. ayuvāv iti kim? daridrāṇam, daridrāyakaḥ. apitīty eva: adaridrām.

luṅi vā (5.3.114)
luṅi parato daridrāter lopo vā bhavati. adaridrīt, adaridrāsīt.

asdādhāṃ hāv ed adviś ca (5.3.115)
aster dādhaś ca hau parata ed bhavati, dviḥprayogaś ca na bhavati. edhi, dehi, dhehi.

liṭy anādeśāder ekahalmadhye 'taḥ (5.3.116)
liṭi parabhūte ādeśa ādir yasyāḥ prakṛter nāsti tasyā akārasyāsahāyayor halor madhye vartamānasya ettvaṃ bhavati, dviḥprayogaś ca na bhavati. reṇatuḥ, reṇuḥ. yematuḥ, yemuḥ. liṭīti kim? yaṃyamyate. anādeśāder iti kim? babhaṇatuḥ, babhaṇuḥ. liṭādeśaviśeṣaṇaṃ kim? nematuḥ, nemuḥ. sehe, sehāte. anaimittike natvasatve iti nāyaṃ liṭy ādeśādiḥ. ekahalmadhya iti kim? tatakṣatuḥ, tatakṣuḥ. ata iti kim? didivatuḥ, didivuḥ. taparaḥ kim? rarāse, rarāsāte. iha prakṛter dviruktau purvasyādeśaḥ prakṛtyādeśa ity ucyate, abhedāt; śasidadipratiṣedhāc ca bhinnarūpādeśo gṛhyate. apitīty eva: ahaṃ papaca, aha.papaṭha.

thalīṭi (5.3.117)
iḍādau thali parato 'nādeśāder ekahalmadhye 'ta ettvaṃ bhavati, adviś ca. pecitha, śekitha. iṭīti kim? papaktha. anādeśāder ity eva: babhaịtha. ekahalmadhya ity eva: tatakṣitha. ata ity eva: didevitha.

tṝphalabhajatrapaḥ (5.3.118)
taratyādīnāṃ liṭy apiti thali ceḍādau parato 'ta ettvaṃ bhavati, adviś ca. teratuḥ, teruḥ; teritha. phelatuḥ, pheluḥ; phelitha. bhejatuḥ, bhejuḥ; bhejitha. trepe, trepāte, trepire. apitīty eva: ahaṃ tatara.

rādho hiṃsāyām (5.3.119)
rādho hiṃsārthasya ya ākāras tasya liṭy apiti thali ceṭi parata ettvaṃ bhavati, adviś ca. aparedhatuḥ, aparedhuḥ; aparedhitha. hiṃsāyām iti kim? ārarādhatuḥ, ārarādhuḥ. apitīty eva: apararādha.

vā jṝbhramatrasām (5.3.120)
jṝprabhṛtīnāṃ liṭy apiti thali ceṭi parato 'ta ed vā bhavati, adviś ca. jeratuḥ, jeruḥ, jeritha; jajaratuḥ, jajaruḥ, jajaritha. bhrematuḥ, bhremuḥ, bhremitha; babhramatuḥ, babhramuḥ, babhramitha. tresatuḥ, tresuḥ, tresitha; tatrasatuḥ, tatrasuḥ, tatrasitha. apitīty eva: ahaṃ jajara.

phaṇādīnāṃ saptānām (5.3.121)
phaṇādīnāṃ saptānāṃ liṭy apiti thali ceḍādau parato 'varṇasya ettvaṃ bhavati vā, adviś ca. pheṇatuḥ, pheṇuḥ, pheṇitha; paphaṇatuḥ, paphaṇuḥ, paphaṇitha. apitīty eva: ahaṃ paphaṇa. saptānām iti kim? dadhvanatuḥ, dadhvanuḥ.

dambhaśranthagranthām (5.3.122)
dambhādīnāṃ liṭy apiti parato 'ta ettvaṃ bhavati, adviś ca. debhatuḥ, debhuḥ. śrethatuḥ, śrethuḥ. grethatuḥ, grethuḥ. apitīty eva: dadambha. dambher nalopasyāsiddhatvāc cārambhaḥ. thalīṭi (5.3.117) iti nivṛttam, tatra nalopābhāvāt.

manipacimacāṃ nāmni (5.3.123)
manyādīnāṃ saṃjñāyām ata ettvaṃ bhavati. Menā, Menakā. pecā, pecakā. mecā, mecakā.

naśo 'ṅi (5.3.124)
naśer aṅi parato 'ta ettvaṃ bhavati. aneśam.

na śasadadavādyadeṅām (5.3.125)
śaser dader vādīnām adeṅvidhānavihitasya cāta ettvaṃ na bhavati. viśaśasatuḥ, viśaśasuḥ, viśaśasitha. dadade, dadadāte, dadadire. vavamatuḥ, vavamuḥ, vavamitha. viśaśaratuḥ, viśaśaruḥ, viśaśaritha. cicayitha, lulavitha. arvantam, arvantāv iti śatrā siddham, arvāṇam, arvāṇāv iti vanipā siddham. Maghavantau, Maghavanta iti matupā siddham, Maghavan niti prakṛtyantaram asti.

yaci aśisuṭi (5.3.126)
yakārādāv ajādau ca śisuḍvarjita ity etad adhikṛtaṃ veditavyam.

pādaḥ pat (5.3.127)
pādantāyāḥ prakṛter yacy aśisuṭi parataḥ pācchabdasya padādeśo bhavati. Vaiyāghrapadyaḥ. dvipadaḥ paśya, dvipadā kṛtam. dvipadikāṃ dadāti. yacīty eva: dvipādbhyām. aśisuṭīty eva: dvipāndi kulāni; dvipādau, dvipādaḥ. svādigrahaṇād akiśoradhenunyāyena: dvipādyati.

vasor va ut (5.3.128)
vaso vakārasya yacy aśisuṭi parata udādeśo bhavati. viduṣaḥ paśya, viduṣā kṛtam. pecuṣaḥ paśya, pecuṣā kṛtam. yacīty eva: vidvadbhyām. aśisuṭīty eva: vidvāṃsau, vidvāṃsaḥ.

śvayuvanmaghonām anaṇādau (5.3.129)
śvādīnām anaṇādau yacy aśisuṭi parato vakārasyodādeśo bhavati. śunaḥ, śunā, śunī. yūnaḥ, yūnā, yūnī. Maghonaḥ, Maghonā, Maghonī. anaṇādāv iti kim? śauvaṃ māṃsam, yauvanaṃ vartate, Māghavanaḥ sthālīpākaḥ. nakāranirdeśaḥ kim? yuvatyā, Maghavatyeti śabdāntaratvāt.

allopo 'naḥ (5.3.130)
anantāyāḥ prakṛter yacy aśisuṭi parato 'to lopo bhavati. rājñaḥ, rājñā. takṣṇaḥ, takṣṇā.

ṣapūrvahandhṛtarājñām aṇi (5.3.131)
ṣapūrvasya hanter Dhṛtarājñaś cāno 'ṇi parato 'llopo bhavati. aukṣṇaḥ, tākṣṇaḥ, bhrauṇaghnaḥ, Dhārtarājñaḥ. eṣām iti kim? sāmanaḥ, vaimanaḥ. aṇīti kim? tākṣaṇyaḥ. kārutvāṇ ṇyaḥ.

ṅiśyor vā (5.3.132)
ṅi śī ity etayoḥ parato 'nantāyāḥ prakṛter ato lopo bhavati. sāmni, sāmani. sāmnī, sāmanī.

na saṃyogād vamaḥ (5.3.133)
na saṃyogād vakārān makārāc ca parasyānantāyā ato lopo bhavati. carmaṇā, carmaṇe. parvaṇā, parvaṇe. saṃyogād iti kim? pratidīvnā, sāmnā. vama iti kim? takṣṇā.

acaḥ (5.3.134)
añcater yacy aśisuṭi parato 'to lopo bhavati. dadhīcaḥ, dadhīcā. madhūcaḥ, madhūcā. prāptyabhāvāt pratiṣedho nānuvartate.

uda īt (5.3.135)
udaḥ parasyāñcater yacy aśisuṭi parato 'ta īdādeśo bhavati. udīcaḥ, udīcā.

ātaḥ (5.3.136)
ākārāntāyāḥ prakṛter yacy aśisuṭi parato lopo bhavati. kīlālapaḥ, kīlālapā. śubhaṃyaḥ, śubhaṃyā. yacīty eva: kīlālapābhyām. aśisuṭīty eva: kīlālapāṃ paśya. kathaṃ khaṭvāḥ paśya, khaṭvayā kṛtam? ṭi cāpaḥ (6.2.43), kulaṭāyā vā (2.4.57) ityādijñāpakāt.

viṃśater ḍiti teḥ (5.3.137)
viṃśater ḍiti parato tiśabdasya lopo bhavati. viṃśatyā krītaḥ, viṃśakaḥ. viṃśaṃ śatam.

antyājādeḥ (5.3.138)
antyo 'j ādir yasya tasya prakṛtyavayavasya ḍiti parato lopo bhavati. trimśakaḥ. kumudvān, naḍvān. upasarajaḥ. ḍitkaraṇasāmarthyād asvādāv ayacy api bhavati.

no 'ṇādau (5.3.139)
aṇādau yaci parato nakārāntāyāḥ prakṛter antyājādilopo bhavati. Āgniśarmiḥ, Auḍulomiḥ. na iti kim? Sātvataḥ. aṇādāv iti kim? śarmaṇā, śarmaṇe.

kalāpyādīnām (5.3.140)
Kalāpin nity evamādīnām aṇādau yaci parato 'ntyājādilopo bhavati. Kalāpinā proktaṃ vedaṃ vidanty adhīyate vā, Kālāpāḥ. Kauthumāḥ. Taitalī Jājalī cācāryau, tatkṛto granthas tacchabdenocyate. tam adhīyate Taitalāḥ, Jājalāḥ. evaṃ Lāṅgalāḥ. Kalāpin - Kuthumin - Taitalin - Jājalin - Lāṅgalin - Brahmacārin - Pīṭhamardin - Sūkaramardin - Suparvan - aśmano vikāre: āśmaḥ; āśmano  'nyaḥ - carmaṇaḥ kośe: cārmaḥ; kośa iti kim? cārmaṇaḥ - śuno 'vayavasaṃkocayoḥ: śauvaṃ māṃsam, śauvaḥ saṃkocaḥ; śauvano 'nyaḥ - asaṃkhyasyānārācchaśvato 'siti: sāyaṃprātikaḥ, paunaḥpunikaḥ. anārācchaśvata iti kim? ārātīyaḥ, śāśvatikaḥ. asitīti kim? śaṃyuḥ, kaṃyuḥ. 

ahnaḥ khe (5.3.141)
ahnaḥ khe parato 'ntyājādilopo bhavati. dve ahnī bhūto, dvyahīnaḥ. tryahīnaḥ. kha iti kim? āhnikaḥ.

asarvāsaṃkhyaikadeśāṭ ṭe (5.3.142)
ṭe parato 'hno 'ntyājādilopo bhavati, na cet sarvaśabdād asaṃkhyād ekadeśavācinaś ca paro bhavati. paramāhaḥ, uttamāhaḥ, puṇyāhaḥ, saṃkhyātāhaḥ. sarvādiparyudāsaḥ kim? sarvāhnaḥ; pratyahnaḥ, nirahnaḥ; pūrvāhṇaḥ, aparāhṇaḥ.

samāhāre (5.3.143)
ahnaḥ samāhāre ṭe parato 'ntyājādilopo bhavati. dve ahanī samāhṛte, dvyahaḥ. trahaḥ.

ekāt (5.3.144)
ekāt parasyāhnaṣ ṭe parato 'ntyājādilopo bhavati. ekāhaḥ.

antikasya tame tādeḥ (5.3.145)
antikaśabdasya tame paratas tāder avayavasya lopo bhavati. antamaḥ.

kāder bahulam (5.3.146)
antikasya tame 'nyatra ca parataḥ kakārāder avayavasya lopo bahulaṃ bhavati. antikatamaḥ, antitamaḥ; antitaḥ, antikataḥ. antike sīdatīty antikasat, antiṣat.

or ot (5.3.147)
uvarṇāntāyāḥ prakṛter yacy aṇādau parato bahulam ottvaṃ bhavati. Bābhravyaḥ, Māṇḍavyaḥ; Aupagavaḥ, Kāpaṭavaḥ. bahulam ity eva: Svāyaṃbhuvaḥ.

ḍhe (5.3.148)
ḍhe parata uvarṇāntāyāḥ prakṛter bahulaṃ lopo bhavati. Kāmaṇḍaleyaḥ, Śaitibāheyaḥ, Mādrabāheyaḥ. bahulam ity eva; Kādraveyaḥ.

yasya (5.3.149)
ivarṇāntāyā avarṇāntāyāś ca prakṛter yacy aṇādau parato bahulaṃ lopo bhavati. Sāṃkṛtyaḥ, Gārgyaḥ, Aitikāyanaḥ, Kāleyaḥ, Dauleyaḥ, Dākṣiḥ, Plākṣiḥ. bahulam ity eva: ūrṇāyuḥ.

ṅyām (5.3.150)
ṅyāṃ parato yasya lopo bhavati. Dākṣī, Plākṣī, kumārī, kiśorī, gaurī.

matsyasya yaḥ (5.3.151)
matsyasya ṅyāṃ parato yakārasya lopo bhavati. matsī.

halo yañādeḥ (5.3.152)
halaḥ parasya yañādiyakārasya ṅyāṃ parato lopo bhavati. Gārgī, saumī. hala iti kim? kārikeyī. yañāder iti kim? vaidyasya bhāryā, vaidyī.

sauryāgastyayoś che ca (5.3.153)
sauryasyāgastyasya ca che ṅyāṃ ca parato yakārasya lopo bhavati. saurīyaḥ, saurī. Āgastīyaḥ, Āgastī. chaṅībhyāṃ yakāraviśeṣaṇād iha na bhavati: Āgastyacarī.

tiṣyapuṣyayor nakṣatre 'ṇi (5.3.154)
tiṣyapuṣyayor nakṣatre vartamānayor aṇi parato yasya lopo bhavati. taiṣī rātriḥ, taiṣam ahaḥ. pauṣī rātriḥ, pauṣam ahaḥ. nakṣatra iti kim? Puṣyasya māṇavakasyedam, Pauṣyam.

āpatyasyānāty aṇādau (5.3.155)
halaḥ parasyāpatye vihitasya yakārasya yacy aṇādāv anāti parato lopo bhavati. Gārgyāṇāṃ samūho, Gārgakam. Vātsakam. āpatyasyeti kim? Sāṃkāśyakaḥ, Kāmpilyakaḥ. anātīti kim? Gārgyāyaṇaḥ. aṇādāv iti kim? Gārgye. hala ity eva: kārikeyiḥ.

kyacvyoḥ (5.3.156)
kyacvyoḥ parato hala uttarasyāpatyasya yakārasya lopo bhavati. gārgīyati, gārgīyate; Gārgībhūtaḥ. āpatyasyety eva: sāṃkāśyīyati, Sāṃkāśyībhūtaḥ. hala ity eva: kārikeyīyati.

bilvakīyādīnām īyaḥ (5.3.157)
Bilvakīyādīnāṃ yacy aṇādau parata īyaśabdasya lopo bhavati. bilvā asyāṃ santi, Bilvakīyā, tasyāṃ bhavāḥ, Bailvakāḥ. evaṃ Vaiṇukāḥ. Bilvakīya - Veṇukīya - Vetasakīya - Vetrakīya - Ikṣukīya - Kāṣṭhakīya - Kapotakīya - Kruñcakīya.

iṣṭhemeyaḥsv antyājādeḥ (5.3.158)
iṣṭhādiṣu parataḥ prakṛter antyājādilopo bhavati. paṭiṣṭhaḥ, paṭīyān, paṭimā. laghiṣṭhaḥ, laghīyān, laghimā. iṣṭhavadbhāvāṇ ṇāv api bhavati: paṭayati, laghayati.

sthūladūrayuvakṣiprakṣudrāṇāṃ yaṇāder yvor eṅ ca (5.3.159)
sthūlādīnām iṣṭhādiṣu yathāsaṃbhavaṃ yaṇāder avayavasya lopo bhavati, ivarṇovarṇayoś ca eṅau bhavataḥ. sthaviṣṭhaḥ, sthavīyān, sthavimā. daviṣṭhaḥ, davīyān, davimā. yaviṣṭhaḥ, yavīyān, yavimā. kṣepiṣṭhaḥ, kṣepīyān, kṣepimā. kṣodiṣṭhaḥ, kṣodīyān, kṣodimā. nāv iṣṭhavadbhāvāt: sthavayati, davayati, yavayati, kṣepayati, kṣodayati.

bahor er bhū ca (5.3.160)
bahoḥ pareṣām iṣṭhādīnām ivarṇasya lopo bhavati, bhū ca bahor ādeśaḥ. bhūyān, bhūmā.

iṣṭhe yik ca (5.3.161)
iṣṭhe parato bahor bhūr ādeśo bhavati, yik cāgamaḥ. bhūyiṣṭhaḥ. ṇāv iṣṭhavadbhāvāt: bhūyayati.

jyāyān (5.3.162)
jyāśabdāt parasyeyasa āttvaṃ nipātyate.

priyasthirasphirorugurubahulatṛpradīrghahrasvavṛddhavṛndārakāṇāṃ prasthasphavaragarabaṃhatrapadrāghahrasvarṣavṛndāḥ (5.3.163)
priyādīnām iṣṭhādiṣu yathāsaṃbhavaṃ prādaya ādeśā bhavanti. preṣṭhaḥ, preyān, premā. stheṣṭhaḥ, stheyān, sthemā. spheṣṭhaḥ, spheyān, sphemā. variṣṭhaḥ, varīyān, varimā. gariṣṭhaḥ, garīyān, garimā. baṃhiṣṭhaḥ, baṃhīyān, baṃhimā. trapiṣṭhaḥ, trapīyān, trapimā. drāghiṣṭhaḥ, drāghīyān, drāghimā. hrasiṣṭhaḥ, hrasīyān, hrasimā. varṣiṣṭhaḥ, varṣīyān, varṣimā. vṛndiṣṭhaḥ, vṛndīyān, vṛndimā. ṇāv iṣṭhavadbhāvāt: prāpayati, sthāpayati, sphāpayati, varayati, garayati, baṃhayati, trapayati, drāghayati, hrasayati, varṣayati, vṛndayati.

ra ṛtaḥ pṛthumṛdukṛśabhṛśadṛḍhaparivṛḍhānām (5.3.164)
pṛthvādīnām ṛkārasyeṣṭhādiṣu pareṣu repho bhavati. prathiṣṭhaḥ, prathīyān, prathimā. mradiṣṭhaḥ, mradīyān, mradimā. kraśiṣṭhaḥ, kraśīyān, kraśimā. bhraśiṣṭhaḥ, bhraśīyān, bhraśimā. draḍhiṣṭhaḥ, draḍhīyān, draḍhimā. parivraḍhiṣṭhaḥ, parivraḍhīyān, parivraḍhimā. ṇāv iṣṭhavadbhāvāt: prathayati, mradayati, kraśayati, bhraśayati, draḍhayati, parivraḍhayati. pṛthvādīnām iti kim? ṛjiṣṭhaḥ, ṛjīyān; kṛcchrayati, kṛtayati.

naikācaḥ (5.3.165)
iṣṭhādiṣu parato yad uktaṃ tad ekāco na bhavati. srajiṣṭhaḥ, srajīyān, srajayati. sruciṣṭhaḥ, srucīyān, srucayati. ekāca iti kim? vasumattamaḥ, vasiṣṭhaḥ.

ake rājanyamanuṣyayūnām (5.3.166)
ake parato rājanyādīnāṃ yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati. rājanyakam, mānuṣyakam. manojñāditvād (4.1.149) vuñ: yauvanikā.

ātmādhvanoḥ khe (5.3.167)
ātmano 'dhvanaś ca khe parato yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati. ātmanīnaḥ, adhvanīnaḥ. kha iti kim? pratyātmam, prādhvam.

abhāvakarmaṇor ano ye (5.3.168)
anantasya ye parato yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati, sa ced bhāvakarmaṇor avihito bhavati. sāmasu sādhuḥ, sāmanyaḥ. brahmaṇyaḥ. abhāvakarmaṇor iti kim? rājño bhāvaḥ karma vā, rājyam. ya iti kim? mahārājaḥ.

aṇi (5.3.169)
aṇi parato 'nantasya yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati. sāmanaḥ, vaimanaḥ.

karmaṇo 'śīle (5.3.170)
karmaṇo 'ṇi parato yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati, śīlaṃ cen na gamyate. kārmaṇaḥ. aśīla iti kim? kārmaḥ. aṇīty eva: kārmukam.

mād varmaṇo 'patye (5.3.171)
mād eva parasya varmaṇa evāpatye 'nantasyāṇi parato yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati. Cākravarmaṇaḥ. mād iti kim? Sautvanaḥ. varmaṇa iti kim? Sauṣāmaḥ.

hitanāmno vā (5.3.172)
Hitanāmno 'patye 'ṇi yad uktaṃ tan neti vā bhavati. Haitanāmanaḥ, Haitanāmaḥ.

brahmaṇo jātau (5.3.173)
brahmaṇo 'patye 'ṇi jātāv abhidheyāyāṃ yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati. brāhmaṇaḥ. jātāv iti kim? brāhmo Manuḥ. apatya iti eva: brāhmī oṣadhiḥ.

ukṣṇaḥ (5.3.174)
ukṣanśabdasyāpatye 'ṇi yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati. Aukṣṇaḥ. punarvidhānād alopaḥ. apatya ity eva: aukṣaṃ padam.

saṃyogād ino 'samūhe (5.3.175)
saṃyogāt paro ya in tadantasyāsamūhe 'ṇi yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati. Śāṅkhinaḥ, Vājriṇaḥ. asamūha iti kim? daṇḍināṃ samūho, dāṇḍam.

gāthividathikeśigaṇipaṇinām (5.3.176)
gāthyādīnām asamūhe 'ṇi yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati. Gāthinaḥ, Vaidathinaḥ, Kaiśinaḥ, Gāṇinaḥ, Pāṇinaḥ. asamūha ity eva: gaṇināṃ samūho, gāṇam.

anapatye ca (5.3.177)
inantasya śeṣasyānapatye 'samūhe cārthe yad uktaṃ tan na bhavati. sāṃkūṭinam, sāṃrāviṇam. sragviṇa idam, srāgviṇam. apatye tu bhavaty eva: Medhāvino 'patyam, Maidhāvaḥ. asamūha ity eva: rathināṃ samūho, rātham.

dāṇḍināyanahāstināyanajaihmāśineyavāsināyanibhrauṇahatyadhaivatyasāravaikṣvākahiraṇmayāni (5.3.178)
Dāṇḍināyanādīni śabdarūpāṇi yathāyogaṃ nipātyante. Daṇḍihastibhyām apatye Naḍāditvāt phaki lopābhāvaḥ: Dāṇḍināyanaḥ, Hāstināyanaḥ. Jihmāśinaḥ Śubhrāditvāḍ ḍhaki Jaihmāśineyaḥ. Vāsino 'gotrād ādaijādyaca (2.4.90) iti phiñ: Vāsināyaniḥ. bhrūṇaghno dhīvnaś ca bhāve ṣyañi tatvam: bhrauṇahatyam, dhaivatyam. Sarayvāṃ bhave 'ṇi yalopaḥ: Sāravaḥ. Ikṣvākor aṇi janapadād añi vā ukāralopaḥ: Ikṣvākor idam, apatyaṃ vā, Aikṣvākaḥ. hiraṇyasya vikāre mayaṭi yalopaḥ: hiraṇmayam.

pañcamasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ samāptaḥ.


yuvor anākāv asaḥ (5.4.1)
yor asakārakasya voś cānākāv ādeśau bhavataḥ. nandanaḥ, gamanam; kārakaḥ, Kācchakaḥ. asa iti kim? kaṃyuḥ, śaṃyuḥ. yuvor iti samāhārasyaikatvād ekavacanam. vikalpānuvṛtter anapuṃsakatvam. yudhabudhādīnāṃ na bhavaty anarthakatvāt, yauter yavayavaka (4.2.3) ityāder jñāpakāt, bhujyur ity auṇādikatvāt (Uṇ. 1.34).

āyaneyinīyīyaḥ phaḍhakhachaghāṃ ṣphādyādīnām (5.4.2)
ṣphādīnām ādibhūtā ye phakārādayas teṣām āyanādaya ādeśā bhavanti. ṣphaḥ: Gārgyāyaṇī. ḍhak: Sauparṇeyī. khaḥ: kulīnaḥ. chaḥ: svasrīyaḥ. ghaḥ: kṣatriyaḥ. ṣphādigrahaṇaṃ kim? phakkati, ḍhaukate. ādigrahaṇaṃ kim? jānudaghnam.

ṭhasyekaḥ (5.4.3)
ṣphādīnāṃ ṭhakārasya ikādeśo bhavati. ākṣikaḥ. ṣphādīnām ity eva: kaṇṭhaḥ. ādīnām ity eva: karmaṭhaḥ.

isusugdorbhyaḥ kaḥ (5.4.4)
is us uk ity evamantāyāḥ prakṛter doḥśabdāc ca parasya ṭhakārasya kādeśo bhavati. sārpiṣkaḥ, dhānuṣkaḥ, Śābarajambukaḥ, mātṛkaḥ, paitṛkaḥ. dorbhyāṃ carati, dauṣkaḥ. āśiṣikaḥ, auṣika ity anarthakatvāl lākṣaṇikatvāc ca na bhavati. āyanādayaś caita upadeśāvasthāyām eva bhavanti nirnimittatvāt, yuc ṭhaj iti cakārasyāntodāttārthatvāc ca.

to 'śaśvataḥ (5.4.5)
takārāntāyāḥ prakṛter aśaśvato vihitasya ṭhasya kādeśo bhavati. audaśvitkaḥ, bhāvatkaḥ. aśaśvata iti kim? śāśvatikaḥ. vihitaviśeṣaṇaṃ kim? māthitikaḥ.

anañsamāse ktvo lyap (5.4.6)
naño 'nyasya ktvāntena samāse ktvo lyab bhavati. prakṛtya, prastutya, prahṛtya. anañ iti kim? akṛtvā. samāsa iti kim? pṛthak kṛtvā, hiruk kṛtvā. anañ iti nañsadṛśasyāsaṃkhyasya grahaṇād iha na bhavati: paramakṛtvā; pītvābhuktakasnātvākālakādiṣv asamāsatvāc ca. upadeśāvasthāyām eva lyab bhavati, ti kiti (5.4.85) iti siddhe jagdhavidhau lyabgrahaṇāt (5.4.86).

ṝta id dhātoḥ (5.4.7)
ṝkārāntasya dhātor idādeśo bhavati. kirati, girati; cikīrṣati, jihīrṣati. dhātor iti kim? mātṝṇām. idaṃ ca jñāpakaṃ lākṣaṇikasyāpi grahaṇāya.

upāntasya (5.4.8)
antasamīpasya ṝkārasyedādeśo bhavati. kīrtayati, kīrtakaḥ. upāntasyeti kim? ṝkārīyati.

ud oṣṭhyāt (5.4.9)
oṣṭhyāt parasya ṝkārasyodādeśo bhavati. prapūrtāḥ piṇḍāḥ. pūḥ, purau, puraḥ. taparaḥ kim? dīrghasya sthāne dīrgho mā bhūt, amū amī iti yathā.

idito num (5.4.10)
idito dhātor num āgamo  bhavati. kuṇḍā, huṇḍā, kuṇḍitā. upadeśāvasthāyām eva num bhavati, nirnimittatvāt, dhātvadhikārāc ca. dhātor ity eva: acaīṣīt.

śe mucādīnām (5.4.11)
śe parato mucādīnāṃ num bhavati. muñcati, lumpati. kathaṃ tṛpati tṛmpati, dṛpati dṛmpatīti? dhātuṣv eva hi dvidhāpāṭhāt.

naśo jhali (5.4.12)
naśer jhalādau parato num bhavati. naṃṣṭā. jhalīti kim? naśanam.

masjo 'ntyāt pūrvaḥ (5.4.13)
masjer antyāt pūrvo jhalādau num bhavati. maṅktā. antyāt pūrva iti kim? saṃyogādilopo yathā syāt. jhalīty eva: majjanam.

jabho 'ci (5.4.14)
jabher ajādau parato num bhavati. jambhayati, jambhakaḥ.

radhaḥ (5.4.15)
rāder ajādau num bhavati. randhayati, randhakaḥ.

iṭi liṭi (5.4.16)
iḍādau liṭy eva parato radher num bhavati. rarandhiva, rarandhima. liṭīti kim? radhitā.

rabho 'śapliṭoḥ (5.4.17)
rabher aśapy aliṭi cājādau parato num bhavati. ārambhaḥ, ārambhakaḥ. aśapliṭor iti kim? ārabhate, ārebhe.

labhaḥ (5.4.18)
labher ajādāv aśapliṭor num bhavati. ālambhaḥ, ālambhakaḥ. aśapliṭor ity eva: ālabhate, ālebhe.

āṅo yi (5.4.19)
āṅaḥ parasya labher yakārādau parato num bhavati. ālambhyā gauḥ.

upāt stutau (5.4.20)
upāt parasya labher yakārādau parataḥ stutau gamyamānāyāṃ num bhavati. upalambhyā bhavatā vidyā. stutāv iti kim? upalabhyam asmād vṛṣalāt kiṃcit.

prādibhyaḥ khalghañoḥ (5.4.21)
prādibhya eva parasya labheḥ khali ghañi ca parato num bhavati. īṣatpralambhaḥ kaṭo bhavatā. upalambhaḥ. prādibhya iti kim? īṣallabhaḥ, lābhaḥ.

na suduraḥ kevalāt (5.4.22)
sudurbhyāṃ kevalābhyāḥ parasya labher num na bhavati. sulabhaḥ, durlabhaḥ. kevalād iti kim? atisulambhaḥ, atidurlabhaḥ.

ciṇṇamor aprāder vā (5.4.23)
prādirahitasya labheś ciṇi ṇamuli ca parato num vā bhavati. alambhi, alābhi. lambhaṃ lambham, lābhaṃ lābhaṃ. aprāder iti kim? prālambhi, pralambhaṃ pralambham.

puṃsuṭy ugitaḥ (5.4.24)
ugitaḥ prakṛteḥ puṃsuṭi parato num bhavati. śreyān, śreyāṃsau, śreyāṃsaḥ, śreyāṃsam, śreyāṃsau. puṃsīti kim? śreyasī kule. suṭīti kim? śreyasaḥ paśya.

añcaḥ (5.4.25)
añcater evogito dhātoḥ suṭi parato num bhavati. prāṅ, prāñcau, prāñcaḥ, prāñcam, prāñcau. añca iti kim? ukhāsrat, parṇadhvat. kathaṃ gomatyateḥ kvip, gomān iti? bhūvādidhātor niyamān num bhaviṣyati.

yujer asamāse (5.4.26)
yujer asamāse suṭi parato num bhavati. yuṅ, yuñjau, yuñjaḥ, yuñjam, yuñjau. asamāsa iti kim? aśvayuk.

śāv ayamaḥ (5.4.27)
yamantād anyasya śau parato num bhavati. śreyāṃsi, mahānti, udaśvinti, kuṇḍāni, vanāni. śāv iti kim? śreyasī kule. ayama iti kim? catvāri, ahāni.

bahūrji bahūrñji (5.4.28)
bahūrjaḥ śau parato 'ntyāt pūrvo numāgamo vā bhavati. bahūrji, bahūrñji.

iko 'ci supi (5.4.29)
igantasyājādau supi parato num bhavati. dadhinī, dadhīni. madhunī, madhūni. napuṃsaka evāyaṃ vidhir bhavati, tatprastāvāt, bhāṣitapuṃskasya ca vāvacanāt. tasmād dīrghībhūtāc chaso naḥ puṃsi (5.1.110) iti liṅgāt, puṃsīti ca natve viśeṣaṇāt striyām api dīrghatvena bhavitavyam, ataḥ pāriśeṣyān napuṃsaka evāyaṃ vidhir bhavati. ika iti kim? kuṇḍe. acīti kim? he trapo. asmād eva vacanād aluki (5.3.3) iti pratiṣedho nāstīty eṅ bhavati. supīti kim? taumburavaṃ cūrṇam.

uktapuṃskasya ṭādau vā (5.4.30)
bhāṣitapuṃskasyegantasya napuṃsakaliṅgasya tṛtīyādāv ajādau parato num vā bhavati. kartṛṇā kulena, kartrā. śucine kulāya, śucaye. uktapuṃskasyeti kim? vāriṇā, vāriṇe. ṭādāv iti kim? grāmaṇinī kule.

asthidadhisakthyakṣṇām anaṅ (5.4.31)
asthyādīnāṃ ṭādāv ajādau supi parato 'naṅādeśo bhavati. asthnā, dadhnā, sakthnā, akṣṇā.

nājjheḥ śatuḥ (5.4.32)
adbhūto jhir yasyāḥ prakrtes tataḥ parasya śatur num bhavati na. dadat, dadhat, jakṣat, jāgrat. ajjher iti kim? lihan.

śau vā (5.4.33)
ajjheḥ parasya śatuḥ śau parato num āgamo vā bhavati. dadanti kulāni. jāgranti kulāni, jāgrati kulāni.

āc chīṅyoḥ (5.4.34)
avarṇāntāt parasya śatuḥ śī ṅī ity etayoḥ parato num vā bhavati. tudantī kule, tudatī kule. tudantī brāhmaṇī, tudatī brāhmaṇī.

śapśyanaḥ (5.4.35)
śapaḥ śyanaś ca parasya śatuḥ śīṅī ity etayoḥ parato num bhavati, nityaṃ punarvidhānāt. pacantī kule, dīvyantī kule. pacantī brāhmaṇī, dīvyantī brāhmaṇī.

sāv anaḍuhaḥ (5.4.36)
sau parato 'naḍuho num bhavati. anaḍvān. sāv iti kim? anaḍvāhau, anaḍvāhaḥ.

diva aut (5.4.37)
divaḥ sau parata aud bhavati. dyauḥ.

pathimathyṛbhukṣām āt (5.4.38)
pathyādīnāṃ sau parata ād bhavati. panthāḥ, manthāḥ, Ṛbhukṣāḥ.

śisuṭy eḥ (5.4.39)
pathyādīnām ikārasya śau suṭi ca parata ād bhavati. bahupanthāni, panthānau, panthānaḥ. bahumanthāni, manthānau, manthānaḥ. bahvṛbhukṣāṇi, Ṛbhukṣāṇau, Ṛbhukṣāṇaḥ.

tho nthaḥ (5.4.40)
pathyādīnāṃ thakārasya śisuṭi parato nthādeśo bhavati. bahupanthāni, panthāḥ. bahumanthāni, manthāḥ.

ino 'ci lopaḥ (5.4.41)
pathyādīnām inśabdasyājādau supi parato lopo bhavati, śisuṭo 'nyatra sāmarthyāt. pathaḥ, pathā. mathaḥ, mathā. Ṛbhukṣaḥ, Ṛbhukṣā.

puṃso 'suṅ (5.4.42)
puṃsaḥ śau suṭi ca parato 'suṅādeśo bhavati. bahupumāṃsi; pumān, pumāṃsau, pumāṃsaḥ, pumāṃsam, pumāṃsau. śisuṭīty eva: puṃsaḥ, puṃsā.

gor auḥ svārthe (5.4.43)
gośabdasya svārthe vartamānasya suṭi parata aukāro bhavati. gauḥ, gāvau, gāvaḥ. svārtha iti kim? he citrago, he citragavaḥ. suṭīty eva: gavā.

sakhyur aśāv ait (5.4.44)
sakhiśabdasya śivarjite suṭi parata aid bhavati. sakhāyau, sakhāyaḥ. aśāv iti kim? atisakhīni. suṭīty eva: sakhīn.

ṛduśanaspurudaṃśo 'nehasāṃ cānaṅ sau (5.4.45)
ṛkārāntasya Uśanaḥprabhṛtīnāṃ ca sakhiśabdasya ca sau parato 'naṅādeśo bhavati. kartā; Uśanā, Purudaṃśā, anehā; sakhā.

na saṃbuddhau (5.4.46)
ṛdādīnāṃ sāv anaṅ na bhavati saṃbodhane. he pitaḥ, he Purudaṃśaḥ, he 'nehaḥ, he sakhe.

vośanasaḥ (5.4.47)
Uśanasaḥ saṃbodhane sāv anaṅ vā bhavati. he Uśanaḥ, he Uśanan.

kruśas tunas tṛc (5.4.48)
kruśaḥ parasya tunaḥ śisuṭi paratas tṛjādeśo bhavati. bahukroṣṭṝṇi; kroṣṭā, kroṣṭārau, kroṣṭāraḥ. śisuṭīty eva: kroṣṭūn.

striyām (5.4.49)
striyāṃ vartamānasya kruśaḥ parasya tunas tṛjādeśo bhavati. kroṣṭrī. pañcabhiḥ kroṣṭrībhiḥ krītai rathaiḥ, pañcakroṣṭṛbhī rathaiḥ. tṛtīyādiṣu tunantasya tṛjantasya ca prayogo bhaviṣyati: kroṣṭunā, kroṣṭrā.

caturanaḍuhor ām (5.4.50)
caturo 'naḍuhaś ca śisuṭi parata ām āgamo bhavati. catvāri, catvāraḥ; priyacatvāḥ, priyacatvārau. anaḍvān, anaḍvāhau; bahvanaḍvāṃhi kulāni. śisuṭīty eva: caturaḥ, anaḍuhaḥ.

am sau saṁbuddhau (5.4.51)
caturo 'naḍuhaś ca sau parataḥ saṃbodhane 'm āgamo bhavati. he priyacatvaḥ, he anaḍvan. sāv iti kim? he anaḍvāhau, he anaḍvāhaḥ. saṃbuddhāv iti kim? anaḍvān.

aṣṭano vā supy āt (5.4.52)
aṣṭanaḥ supi parata ād vā bhavati. aṣṭābhiḥ, aṣṭabhiḥ. supīti kim? aṣṭakaḥ saṃghaḥ. alukīty eva: aṣṭa.

rāyo hali (5.4.53)
raiśabdasya halādau supi parata ād bhavati. rābhyām, rābhiḥ. halīti kim? rāyau, rāyaḥ. supīty eva: raitvam, raitā.

yuṣmadasmador anādeśe (5.4.54)
anādeśe supi parato yuṣmadasmador ād bhavati. yuvābhyām, āvābhyām. yuṣmābhiḥ, asmābhiḥ. yuṣmāsu, asmāsu. anādeśa iti kim? yuṣmat, asmat.

auśasamsu (5.4.55)
aukāre śasy ami ca parato yuṣmadasmador ād bhavati. yuvāṃ tiṣṭhathaḥ, āvāṃ tiṣṭhāvaḥ. yuvāṃ paśya, āvāṃ paśya. yuṣmān, asmān. tvām, mām.

yo 'ci (5.4.56)
ajādau supi parato yuṣmadasmador yakārādeśo bhavati. tvayā, mayā. tvayi, mayi. yuvayoḥ, āvayoḥ. anādeśa ity eva: tvat, mat.

śeṣe lopo 'daḥ (5.4.57)
yatra nāttvaṃ na yakāras tasmin supi parato yuṣmadasmador acchabdasya lopo bhavati. tvam, aham. yūyam, vayam. tubhyam, mahyam. yuṣmabhyam, asmabhyam. tvat, mat. yuṣmat, asmat. tava, mama. yuṣmākam, asmākam.

māntasya yuvāvau dvivacane (5.4.58)
dvivacane vartamānayor yuṣmadasmador māntasya śabdarūpasya yuvāvau bhavataḥ. yuvām, āvām. yuvābhyām, āvābhyām. yuvayoḥ, āvayoḥ. māntasyety ayam adhikāraḥ.

yūyavayau jasi (5.4.59)
yuṣmadasmador jasi parato māntasya yūyavayau bhavataḥ. yūyam, vayam.

tvāhau sau (5.4.60)
sau parato yuṣmadasmados tva aha ity etāv ādeśau bhavataḥ. tvam, aham.

tubhyamahyau ṅayi (5.4.61)
ṅasi parato yuṣmadasmados tavamamau bhavataḥ. tava, mama.

tavamamau ṅasi (5.4.62)
ṅasi parato yuṣmadasmados tavamamau bhavataḥ. tava, mama.

tvamāv ekasmin (5.4.63)
ekasmin narthe vartamānayor yuṣmadasmados tva ma ity etau bhavataḥ. tvām, mām. tvayā, mayā. tvat, mat. tvayi, mayi. tvadīyaḥ, madīyaḥ. tvatputraḥ, matputraḥ.

tricaturoḥ striyāṃ tisṛcatasṛ (5.4.64)
tricaturoḥ striyāṃ vartamānayoḥ supi paratas tisṛ catasṛ ity etāv ādeśau bhavataḥ. tisṛbhiḥ, catasṛbhiḥ.

tisṛkā (5.4.65)
Tiṣṛketi saṃjñāyāṃ nipātyate. Tisṛkā nāma grāmaḥ.

ṛto ro 'ci (5.4.66)
tricaturor ṛtaḥ supy ajādau parato ro bhavati. tisraḥ, catasraḥ.

jarāyā jaras vā (5.4.67)
jarāśabdasyājādau supi parato jarasādeśo bhavati vā. jarasā dantāḥ śīryante, jarayā vā.

tyadāṃ tasādiṣu cā dver aḥ (5.4.68)
tyadādīnāṃ dviparyantānāṃ supi tasādiṣu ca parato 'kāro bhavati. syaḥ, tyau, tye. saḥ, tau, te. tataḥ, tatra, tadā, tathā. ā dver iti kim? bhavān. tasādiṣu ceti kim? tyadīyaḥ. alukīty eva: tat, yat.

kimaḥ kaḥ (5.4.69)
kimas tasādiṣu supi ca parataḥ kādeśo bhavati. kaḥ, kau, ke; kadā, kathā, karhi.

taḥ saḥ sau (5.4.70)
tyadādīnāṃ takārasya sau parataḥ sakārādeśo bhavati, syaḥ, saḥ, eṣaḥ. sāv iti kim? tau.

asāv asuko 'sakau (5.4.71)
ete śabdā adasaḥ sau tadantasya nipātyante. asau. sākackasya: asukaḥ, asakau.

idam ayam iyam (5.4.72)
ete śabdā idamaḥ sau tadantasya liṅgatraye nipātyante. ayam, iyam, idam.

do maḥ (5.4.73)
idamo dakārasya supi parato makāro bhavati. imau, ime.

ṭausy ako 'naḥ (5.4.74)
ṭākāre osi ca parato 'kakārasyedamo 'nādeśo bhavati. anena, anayoḥ. akaiti kim? imakena.

haly aś (5.4.75)
halādau supi parata idamo 'śādeśo bhavati. ebhiḥ, ābhyām. aka ity eva: imakaiḥ.

etasya cānvādeśe dvitīyāyāṃ cainaḥ (5.4.76)
etacchabdasya ya etaśabdas tasyedamaś ca kathitānukathanaviṣaye dvitīyāyāṃ vibhaktau ṭausi ca parata enādeśo bhavati. etaṃ chāttraṃ vedam adhyāpaya, atho enaṃ vyākaraṇam adhyāpaya. etat kuṇḍam ānaya, atho enat parivartaya. etau chāttrau vedam adhyāpaya, atho enau vyākaraṇam adhyāpaya. etāṃś chāttrān vedam adhyāpaya, atho enān vyākaraṇam adhyāpaya. etena cchāttreṇa rātrir adhītā, atho enena nipuṇam adhītam. etayoś chāttrayoḥ śobhanaṃ śīlam, atho enayoḥ prabhūtaṃ svam. etayor grāmayoḥ sukham avasāma, atho enayoḥ samyag yajāmahe. evam idamo 'pi yojyam, ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ: idaṃ kuṇḍam ānaya, atho enaṃ parivartayeti. makārānta eva bhavati. tṛtīyādiṣu tratasoś cedama evānvādeśe 'pi prayogo bhaviṣyati. kuto 'taḥ (4.3.8), atra (4.3.11) iti nipātanāt siddham.

panniśmāshṛdyūṣandoṣañ śasādau vā (5.4.77)
śasādau supi parataḥ pādādīnāṃ sthāne padādaya ādeśā vā bhavanti. padbhyām, pādābhyām. niśi, niśāyām. māsi, māse. hṛdi, hṛdaye. yuṣṇā, yūṣeṇa. doṣṇā, doṣā. śasādāv iti kim? pādaḥ, niśā, māsaḥ, hṛdayam, yūṣaḥ, doḥ.

liḍāśīrliṅatiṅśiti (5.4.78)
liṭy āśīrliṅy atiṅy aśitīti ca prāk tiṅgrahaṇād (5.4.173) etad adhikṛtaṃ veditavyam.

aster bhūḥ (5.4.79)
aster liḍādiṣu bhūr ādeśo bhavati. babhūva, bhūyāt, bhavitā. lukā nirdeśaḥ kim? asyater mā bhūt: asitā. kathaṃ kārayāmāsa? kṛbhvastibhyo liḍanuprayogavacanāt (1.1.51). liḍādiṣv ity eva: syāt, asti, san.

bruvo vac (5.4.80)
bruvo liḍādiṣu parato vacādeśo bhavati. uvāca, ūce, ucyāt, vaktā. liḍādiṣv ity eva: brūyāt, bravīti, bruvan.

cakṣaḥ khyañ (5.4.81)
cakṣer liḍādiṣu khyāñādeśo bhavati. khyāyāt, khyātā. liḍādiṣv ity eva: ācakṣīta, ācaṣṭe, ācakṣāṇaḥ.

vā liṭi (5.4.82)
liṭi parataś cakṣaḥ khyāñādeśo vā bhavati. ācakhyau, ācakhye; ācacakṣe.

nāsanavarjaneṣu (5.4.83)
asy ane ca parato varjane cārthe cakṣaḥ khyāñādeśo na bhavati. nṛcakṣāḥ, vicakṣaṇaḥ, parisaṃcakṣyaḥ. kathaṃ vyākhyānam? khyāter bhaviṣyati.

ajer vy ayughañapkyeṣu (5.4.84)
ajer liḍādiṣu vībhāvo bhavati, yu ghañ ap kyap etān varjayitvā. vivāya, vīyāt, pravetā, vītaḥ, vītavān. ayughañapkyeṣv iti kim? prājanam, samājaḥ, udajaḥ, samajyā. kathaṃ pravayaṇam? vī dhātvantaram.

ti kity ado jagdhaḥ (5.4.85)
takārādau kiti parato 'do  jagdhādeśo  bhavati. jagdhaḥ, jagdhvā. tīti kim? adyate. kitīti kim? attā.

lyapi (5.4.86)
atter lyapi parato jagdhādeśo bhavati. prajagdhya. ti kitīti siddhe lyapi punarvacanāl liṅgād upadeśāvasthāyām eva lyab bhavati. tena hitvadattvāttvettvadīrghatvaśūṣiṭo na bhavanti: hitvā, pradhāya. dattvā, pradāya. khātvā, prakhanya. sthitvā, prasthāya. śāntvā, praśamya. pṛṣṭvā, āpṛcchyā. dyūtvā, pradīvya. devitvā, pradīvya.

luṅsanajghañapsu ghasḷḥ (5.4.87)
luṅi sany aci ghañy api ca parato 'tter ghasḷādeśo bhavati. aghasat, jighatsati, praghasaḥ, ghāsaḥ, vighasaḥ. dhātvantareṇa siddhe 'dinivṛttyarthaṃ vacanam. liṭi tu dvayam api bhavati: āda, jaghāsa.

veño liṭi vay vā (5.4.88)
veño liṭi parato vayādeśo vā bhavati. uvāya, vavau.

hano vadha liṅi (5.4.89)
hanter liṅi parato vadhādeśo bhavati. vadhyāt. āśiṣīty eva: hanyāt.

luṅi (5.4.90)
luṅi parato hanter vadhādeśo bhavati. avadhīt. vadher adantatvād ād na bhavati.

taṅi vā (5.4.91)
luṅi taṅbhūte parato hanter vadhādeśo vā bhavati. āvadhiṣṭa, āhata.

eter gāḥ (5.4.92)
iṇa ikaś ca luṅi parato gādeśo bhavati. agāt, adhyagāt.

ṇau gam abodhe (5.4.93)
abodhe vartamānasya iṇa ikaś ca ṇau parato gamādeśo bhavati. gamayati grāmam. adhigamayati priyām. abodha iti kim? arthān saṃpratyāpayati.

sani (5.4.94)
iṇa ikaś ca sani parato gamādeśo bhavati. jigamiṣati grāmam. adhijigamiṣati priyām. abodha ity eva: arthān saṃpratīṣiṣati.

iṅaḥ (5.4.95)
iṅaḥ sani parato gamādeśo bhavati. adhijigāṃsate vidyām.

gāṅ liṭi (5.4.96)
liṭi parata i˙õ gāṅādeśo bhavati. adhijage.

vā luṅlṛṅoḥ (5.4.97)
luṅi lṛṅi ca parata iṅo gāṅādeśo bhavati vā. adhyagīṣṭa, adhyaiṣṭa. adhyagīṣyata, adhyaiṣyata. 

ṇau saṃścaṅoḥ (5.4.98)
ṇau sanpare caṅpare ca parata iṅo gāṅādeśo vā bhavati. adhijigāpayiṣati, adhyāpipayiṣati. adhyajīgapat, adhyāpipat. saṃścaṅor iti kim? adhyāpayati.

valāder iṭ (5.4.99)
valāder liṭa āśīrliṅo 'tiṅo 'śitaś ca iḍāgamo bhavati. lulavitha, laviṣīṣṭa, lavitā. tiṅsadṛśasya grahaṇāt svādīnāṃ na bhavati: lūbhyām, lūbhiḥ.

graho 'syāliṭīt (5.4.100)
grahaḥ parasyāsyeṭo 'liṭi parata īkāro bhavati. grahītā. asyeti kim? ciṇvadiṭo (5.3.73) mā bhūt: grāhiṣyate. aliṭīti kim? jagṛhiva, jagṛhima.

vṝto vā (5.4.101)
vṛṅvṛñor ṝkārāntāc ca parasyeṭa īdādeśo vā bhavati. varītā, varitā. prāvarītā, prāvaritā. āstarītā, āstaritā.

na liṅi (5.4.102)
liṅi parato vṝtaḥ parasyeṭa īttvaṃ na bhavati. variṣīṣṭa, prāvariṣīṣṭa, āstariṣīṣṭa.

sicy ataṅi (5.4.103)
ataṅpare sici parato vṝtaḥ parasyeṭa īttvaṃ na bhavati. prāvāriṣṭām, āstāriṣṭām. ataṅīti kim? avarīṣṭa, avariṣṭa.

iṭ sano vā (5.4.104)
vṝtaḥ parasya sana iḍāgamo vā bhavati. vivariṣate, vuvūrṣate. prāvivariṣati, prāvuvūrṣati. nipipariṣati, nipupūrṣati.

liṅsicos taṅi (5.4.105)
vṝtaḥ parasya liṅaḥ sicaś ca taṅviṣaye iḍ vā bhavati. variṣīṣṭa, vṛṣīṣṭa. āstariṣīṣṭa, āstīrṣīṣṭa. avariṣṭa, avṛta. āstariṣātām, āstīrṣātām.

ṛtaḥ saṃyogādeḥ (5.4.106)
ṛkārāntāt saṃyogādeḥ parayor liṅsicos taṅi iḍ vā bhavati. smariṣīṣṭa, smṛṣīṣṭa. asmariṣātām, asmṛṣātām. aupadeśikasaṃyogagrahaṇād iha na bhavati: saṃskṛṣīṣṭa, samaskṛta.

svṛsūṅūditaḥ (5.4.107)
svarateḥ sūteḥ sūyater ūditaś ca parasya valāder iḍ vā bhavati. svaritā, svartā. savitā, sotā. mārjitā, mārṣṭā. anubandhaḥ kim? suvateḥ, savitā. kathaṃ vidhotā, vidhaviteti? dhuvā dhūñā ca siddham.

radhādibhyaḥ (5.4.108)
radha ity evamādibhyaḥ parasya valāder iḍ vā bhavati. radhitā, raddhā. naśitā, naṃṣṭā. tarpitā, traptā. darpitā, draptā. drohitā, drogdhā. mohitā, mogdhā. snohitā, snogdhā. snehitā, snegdhā. liṭi srādiniyamāt (5.4.158) paratvād iṭ: rarandhiva, rarandhima.

niṣkuṣaḥ (5.4.109)
niṣkuṣaḥ parasya valāder iḍ vā bhavati. niṣkoṣitā, niṣkoṣṭā.

tatavatoḥ (5.4.110)
niṣkuṣaḥ parayoḥ ktaktavatvor iḍ bhavati, nityaṃ punarvidhānāt, yato 'patiniṣkuṣo vā (5.4.140) iti tatrāvacanāt. niṣkuṣitaḥ, niṣkuṣitavān.

pūkliśas tvaś ca (5.4.111)
puvaḥ kliśaś ca parayoḥ ktaktavatvoḥ ktvaś ca iḍ vā bhavati. uttaratra nityārtham, vacanād iṭ. pavitvā, pūtvākliśitvā, kliṣṭvā. pavitaḥ, pavitavān; pūtaḥ, pūtavān. kliśitaḥ, kliśitavān; kliṣṭaḥ, kliṣṭavān.

vasakṣudha iṭ (5.4.112)
vasikṣudhibhyāṃ parayoḥ ktaktavatvoḥ ktvaś ca iḍ āgamo bhavati. uṣitvā, uṣitaḥ, uṣitavān. kṣudhitvā. kṣudhitaḥ, kṣudhitavān. vaster iḍ asty eva.

añco ne (5.4.113)
nakāre saty añcateḥ parasya ktvaḥ ktaktavatvoś ca iḍ bhavati. añcitvā jānu juhoti. añcitam iva śiro vahati. añcitavān. nāñcaḥ pūjāyām (5.3.50) iti nalopābhāvaḥ. na iti kim? udaktam udakaṃ kūpāt.

lubha ākule (5.4.114)
lubheḥ parayoḥ ktaktavatvoḥ ktvaś cākule gamyamāna iḍ bhavati. vilubhitāḥ keśāḥ. vilubhitavān. ākula iti kim? lubdho vṛṣalaḥ.

jṝṣas tvaḥ (5.4.115)
jṝṣaḥ parasya ktvā ity etasya iḍ bhavati. jaritvā, jarītvā.

vraścitvā (5.4.116)
vraścitvety ayaṃ śabdo nipātyate.

udito vā (5.4.117)
uditaḥ parasya ktvā ity etasya iḍ vā bhavati. śamitvā, śāntvā.

tīṣusahalubharuṣariṣaḥ (5.4.118)
icchatyādibhyaḥ parasya takārāder valāder iḍ vā bhavati. eṣitā, eṣṭā. sahitā, soḍhā. lobhitā, lobdhā. roṣitā, roṣṭā. reṣitā, reṣṭā. tīti kim? sahiṣyate. iṣu ity utā nirdeśād iṣyater iṣṇāteś ca na bhavati: preṣitā. pañcamī tīti saptamyāḥ ṣaṣṭhīṃ prakalpayati parabalīyastvāt.

sanīvantardhabhrasjadambhuśrisvṛyūrṇubharajñapisanitanipatidaridraḥ (5.4.119)
ivantād ṛdhādibhyaś ca parasya sana iḍ vā bhavati. dideviṣati, dudyūṣati. ardidhiṣati, īrtsati. bibhrajjiṣati, bibhrakṣati. didambhiṣati, dhipsati. śiśrayiṣati, śiśrīṣati. sisvariṣati, susvūrṣati. yiyaviṣati, yuyūṣati. prorṇunaviṣati, prorṇunūṣati. bibhariṣati, bubhūrṣati. śapā nirdeśād anyasya na bhavati: bubhūrṣati. jñīpsati, jijñapayiṣati. sisaniṣati, siṣāsati. titaniṣati, titaṃsati. pipatiṣati, pitsati. didaridriṣati, didaridrāsati.

sy asici kṛtacṛtacchṛdatṛdanṛtaḥ (5.4.120)
kṛtādibhyaḥ parasya sakārāder asica iḍ vā bhavati. kartiṣyati, kartsyati. cartiṣyati, cartsyati. chardiṣyati, chartsyati. tardiṣyati, tartsyati. nartiṣyati, nartsyati. sīti kim? kartitā. asicīti kim? akartiṣṭām.

aniṅgamer iṭ (5.4.121)
aniṅādeśād gameḥ parasya sakārāder iḍ bhavati. gamiṣyati, jigamiṣati, jigamiṣitā, saṃjigamiṣitā. aniṅgamer iti kim? adhijigāṃsitā.

na taṅānaiḥ (5.4.122)
taṅānaiḥ saha prayoge gameḥ parasya sakārāder iḍ na bhavati. saṃjigaṃsate, saṃjigaṃsamānaḥ. samo gamṛchi (1.4.71) ityādinā taṅ. saṃgaṃsyate, saṃgaṃsyamānaḥ, saṃgaṃsīṣṭa.

vṛdbhya iṭ (5.4.123)
vṛtādibhyaḥ parasya sakārādes taṅānair eva saha prayoge iḍ āgamo bhavati. vartiṣyate, vartiṣyamāṇaḥ; vivartiṣate, vivartiṣamāṇaḥ. vardhiṣyate, vardhiṣyamāṇaḥ; vivardhiṣate, vivardhiṣamāṇaḥ. taṅānair ity eva: vartsyati, vivṛtsati, vivṛtsitā.

tāsaś ca kḷpaḥ (5.4.124)
kḷpaḥ parasya tāsaḥ sakārādeś ca taṅānair eva saha prayoge iḍ bhavati. kalpitāse; kalpiṣyate, cikalpiṣate. taṅānair ity eva: kalptā, kalpsyati, cikḷpsati, cikḷpsitā.

na snoḥ (5.4.125)
taṅānaiḥ saha prayoge snoḥ parasya tāsaḥ sakārādeś ca iḍ na bhavati. prasnoṣyate, prasnoṣyamāṇaḥ, prasnotāse. taṅānair ity eva: prasnavitā.

kramaḥ (5.4.126)
taṅānaiḥ saha prayoge kramaḥ parasya tāsaḥ sakārādeś ca iḍ na bhavati. prakraṃsyate, prakraṃsyamānaḥ, prakrantāse. taṅānair ity eva: kramitā. 

taṅviṣayāt kartary atiṅaḥ (5.4.127)
taṅviṣayāt kramaḥ parasya kartṛvṛtter atiṅa iḍ na bhavati. prakrantā. taṅviṣayād iti kim? kramitā. kartarīti kim? prakramitum, prakramitavyam. atiṅa iti kim? pracakramiṣe.

vaśi (5.4.128)
vaśāder atiṅa iḍ na bhavati. īśvaraḥ, bhāsvaraḥ; dīpraḥ; bhasma; rakṣṇaḥ, yācñā; khaṇḍaḥ, daṇḍaḥ. atiṅa ity eva: jagmiva.

ter agrahādibhyaḥ (5.4.129)
grahādivarjitebhyaḥ parasya ter iḍ na bhavati. tantiḥ, rantiḥ, vantiḥ. kathaṃ saktuḥ, pattram, hastaḥ, kāṣṭham, kukṣiḥ, ikṣuḥ, tasaraḥ, śalkaḥ, vatsa iti? auṇādikā ete, yathā garbhaḥ, darbhaḥ, gulphaḥ, śarkaretyādi. grahādiinrāsaḥ kim? nigṛhītiḥ, upasnihitiḥ, nikucitiḥ, nipaḥtitiḥ. ākṛtigaṇatvāt prabhaṇitir ityādi.

ekāco 'śviśriḍīśīṅūyvādiṣaṭkāt (5.4.130)
ekācaḥ śviśriḍīśīṅbhir ūdantair yautyādibhiś ca ṣaḍbhir varjitād iḍ na bhavati. yātā, cetā, netā, stotā, kartā. ekaca iti kim? daridritā, ādīdhitā, vevitā, prorṇavitā, jāgaritā. śvayatyādiparyudāsaḥ kim? śvayitā, śrayitā, ḍayitā, śayitā; lavitā; yavitā, navitā, kṣṇavitā, prasnavitā, kṣavitā, ravitā. ṣaṭkād iti kim? kotā. śvayatyādiparyudāsād uttaratra halantagrahaṇāc ceha na bhavati: paṭhitā. kathaṃ varitā, prāvaritā, āstariteti? vṝto vā, na liṅi (5.4.101, 102) iti vacanāt.

sidhibudhisvidimanipuṣaśliṣaḥ śyanā (5.4.131)
sidhyatyādibhyaḥ śyanopalakṣitebhyaḥ parasya valāder iḍ na bhavati. seddhā, boddhā, svettā, mantā, poṣṭā, śleṣṭā. śyaneti kim? sedhitā, bodhitā, sveditā, manitā, poṣitā, śleṣitā.

vider alukaḥ (5.4.132)
vider alugvikaraṇāt parasya valāder iḍ na bhavati. vettā. aluka iti kim? veditā śāstrāṇām.

yaralād bhaḥ (5.4.133)
yaralebhyaḥ paro yo bhakāras tadantāt parasya valāder iḍ na bhavati. yabdhā, rabdhā, labdhā. yaralād iti kim? umbhitā. bha iti kim? lagitā.

yaranagān maḥ (5.4.134)
yaranagādibhyaḥ paro yo makāras tadantāt parasya valāder iḍ na bhavati. yantā, rantā, praṇantā, gantā.

śakādibhyaḥ (5.4.135)
śaka ity evamādibhyaḥ parasya valāder iḍ āgamo na bhavati. śaktā, ghastā, vastā. śakyater vasteś ceḍ asty eva: śakitā, vasitā. śakḷghasḷvasatihanibhyaḥ - pacivaciricivicisicimuciprachaḥ - diśidṛśiviśiliśiriśiruśimṛśispṛśibhyaḥ - kruśo daṃśaḥ - tyajiyajiyujirujinijivijibhujibhajisṛjisañjirañjibhañjibhyaḥ - svañjimasjibhrasjibhyaḥ - ruhaduhadihalihamihanahadahavahaḥ - adihadiśadisaditudinudibhidichidikṣudipadikhidiskandaḥ - tapatipaśapavapalipalupasṛpasvapāpakṣipachupaḥ - śuṣikṛṣipiṣiviṣiśiṣibhyaḥ - tuṣitviṣiduṣidviṣibhyaḥ - vyadhiyudhirudhiśudhibandhikrudhikṣudheḥ - rādhisādhibhyāṃ ca.

śryugūrṇoḥ kitaḥ (5.4.136)
śrayater ugantād ekāca ūrṇoteṣ ca parasya kito valāder iḍ na bhavati. śritvā, śritaḥ. yutvā, yutaḥ. lūtvā, lūnaḥ. vṛtvā, vṛtaḥ. tīrtvā, tīrṇaḥ. ūrṇutvā, ūrṇutaḥ. ekāca ity eva: jāgaritaḥ. kita iti kim? lavitā.

sano grahaguhaś ca (5.4.137)
grahiguhibhyām ugantāc ca parasya sana iḍ na bhavati. jighṛkṣati, jughukṣati; lulūṣati, pupūṣati. śvayater ūrṇoter yauter vṝtaś ca parasya sana iḍ vibhāṣoktaḥ (5.4.119, 101).

svārthe (5.4.138)
svārthikasya sana iḍ na bhavati. titikṣate, cikitsati, jugupsate.

śvīditas tatavatoḥ (5.4.139)
śvayater īditaś ca parayos tatavator iḍ na bhavati. śūnaḥ, śūnavān. olasjī: lagnaḥ, lagnavān.

yato 'pater vā (5.4.140)
yasmād iḍ vā vihitas tataḥ pativarjitāt parayos tatavator iḍ na bhavati. sūtaḥ, sūtavān. apater iti kim? patitaḥ, patitavān. ekāca ity eva: daridritaḥ. kathaṃ viditaḥ? viśisahacaritasya vidaviśa (5.4.166) iti grahaṇāt.

āditaḥ (5.4.141)
āditaḥ parayos tatavator iḍ na bhavati. minnaḥ, minnavān.

bhāvārambhayor vā (5.4.142)
bhāve tadārambhe ca tatavator iḍ vā na bhavati. minnam, meditam. praminnaḥ, prameditaḥ. ādita ity eva: gatam.

japivamaḥ (5.4.143)
japivamibhyāṃ parayos tatavator iḍ vā na bhavati. japtaḥ, japitaḥ. vāntaḥ, vamitaḥ.

vyāṅaḥ śvasaḥ (5.4.144)
vipūrvād āṅpūrvāc ca śvaseḥ parayos tatavator iḍ vā na bhavati. viśvastaḥ, viśvasitaḥ. āśvastaḥ, āśvasitaḥ. vyāṅa iti kim? niḥśvasitaḥ, ucchvasitaḥ.

kṣubdhasvāntadhvāntaṃ manthamanastamaḥ (5.4.145)
kśubdhādayo manthādiṣv artheṣu nipātyante. kṣubdho manthaḥ. svāntaṃ manaḥ. dhvāntaṃ tamaḥ. samānādhikaraṇaṃ kim? kṣubhitaṃ manthena, svanitaṃ manasā, dhvanitaṃ tamasā.

viribdhaphāṇṭabāḍhamliṣṭāni svarānāyāsabhṛśāspaṣṭeṣu (5.4.146)
viribdhādayaḥ svarādiṣu gamyamāneṣu nipātyante. viribdhaḥ svaraś cet, virebhitam anyat. phāṇṭam anāyāsanirjātaṃ cet. sadyo 'bhiṣutoddhṛtauṣadhaṃ dravadravyam evocyate. phāṇitam anyat. bāḍhaṃ bhṛśaṃ cet, bāhitam anyat. mliṣṭam avispaṣṭaṃ cet, mlechitam anyat.

dhṛṣaśasaḥ prāgalbhye (5.4.147)
dhṛṣiśasibhyāṃ parayos tatavatoḥ prāgalbhya eveḍ na bhavati. dhṛṣṭaḥ, viśastaḥ. prāgalbhya iti kim? dharṣitaḥ, viśasitaḥ.

dṛḍhaḥ sthūlabalinoḥ (5.4.148)
dṛḍha iti sthūle balavati ca nipātyate. dṛḍhaḥ. dṛhitaṃ dṛṃhitaṃ cānyat.

prabhau parivṛḍhaḥ (5.4.149)
parivṛḍha iti prabhau nipātyate. parivṛṃhitam anyat.

kṛcchragahanayoḥ kaṣaḥ (5.4.150)
kṛcchre gahane cārthe kaṣateḥ parayos tatavator iḍ na bhavati. kaṣṭo 'gniḥ. kaṣṭāḥ parvatāḥ. kaṣitam anyatra.

ghuṣer aviśabdane (5.4.151)
viśabdanād anyatra ghuṣeḥ parayos tatavator iḍ na bhavati. ghuṣṭā rajjuḥ. aviśabdana iti kim? avaghuṣitaṃ vākyam āha. ato liṅgād vā ṇic. tena jughuṣuḥ Puṣyamāṇavā iti siddhaṃ bhavati.

saṃniver ardaḥ (5.4.152)
samādipūrvād ardateḥ parayos tatavator iḍ na bhavati. samarṇaḥ, nyarṇaḥ, vyarṇaḥ. saṃniver iti kim? arditaḥ.

abher avidūre (5.4.153)
abheḥ parād ardateḥ parayos tatavator avidūre gamyamāna iḍ na bhavati. abhyarṇā śarat. avidūra iti kim? abhyarditaḥ.

ṇer vṛttaṃ granthe (5.4.154)
vṛter ṇyantasya kte parato granthaviṣaye vṛttam iti nipātyate. vṛttaṃ pārāyaṇaṃ Devadattena. vṛttaṃ pārāyaṇe. vartitam anyat.

vā dāntaśāntapūrṇadastaspaṣṭacchannajñaptāḥ (5.4.155)
ṇyantānām ete kte parato vā nipātyante. dāntaḥ, damitaḥ. śāntaḥ, śamitaḥ. pūrṇaḥ, pūritaḥ. dastaḥ, dāsitaḥ. spaṣṭaḥ,spāśitaḥ. channaḥ, chāditaḥ. jñaptaḥ, jñapitaḥ.

ruṣahṛṣāmatvarasaṃghuṣāsvanaḥ (5.4.156)
ruṣādibhyaḥ parayos tatavator iḍ vā na bhavati. ruṣṭaḥ, ruṣitaḥ. hṛṣṭaḥ, hṛṣitaḥ. hṛṣer lomasu vismitapratighātayor iti ca na vaktavyam, anyatrāpi darśanād arthānyatve ca, vyavasthitavibhāṣayā vā. hṛṣṭāḥ keśāḥ, hṛṣitāḥ keśāḥ. hṛṣtā dantāḥ, hṛṣitā dantāḥ. hṛṣṭaṃ lomabhiḥ, hṛṣitaṃ lomabhiḥ. abhyāntaḥ, abhyamitaḥ. tūrṇaḥ, tvaritaḥ. saṃghuṣṭaḥ, saṃghuṣitaḥ. āsvāntaḥ, āsvanitaḥ. aviśabdane manasi ca paratvād anenaiva bhavitavyam. apacita iti cinoter bhaviṣyati, tata eva pūjā pratīyate. apacāyita iti cāyater bhaviṣyati.

apacitiḥ (5.4.157)
apapūrvasya cāyeḥ ktini parataś cibhāvo nipātyate. apacitiḥ. cāyṛnivṛttyarthaṃ vacanam.

sṛbhṛvṛstudrusruśruvo liṭaḥ (5.4.158)
srādibhya eva parasya valāder liṭa iḍ na bhavati. sasṛva, sasṛma. babhṛva, babhṛma, babhṛvahe, babhṛmahe. vavṛva, vavṛma, vavṛvahe, vavṛmahe. vṛṅvṛñor valādilakṣaṇa eva pratiṣidhyate. tuṣṭuva, tuṣṭuma. dudruva, dudruma. susruva, susruma. śuśruva, śuśruma. srādibhya iti kim? peciva, pecima. śekiva, śekima.

kṛño 'suṭaḥ (5.4.159)
asuṭkāt karoteḥ parasya liṭa iḍ na bhavati. cakṛva, cakṛma. srādiniyamāt prāptasya pratiṣedhaḥ. asuṭa iti kim? saṃcaskariva, saṃcaskarima.

ṛtas tāsi nityāniṭas thalaḥ (5.4.160)
ṛdantāt tāsi nityāniṭaḥ parasya thala iḍ na bhavati. hartā: jahartha. ṛta iti kim? bhettā: bibheditha. tāsīti kim? vṛtaḥ: vavaritha. nityam iti kim? svartā, svaritā: sasvaritha. aniṭa iti kim? jāgaritā: jajāgaritha. thala iti kim? jahriva, jahrima. aco vā (5.4.161) iti prāptasya pratiṣedhaḥ.

aco vā (5.4.161)
ajantāt tāsi nityāniṭaḥ parasya thala iḍ vā na bhavati. yātā: yayātha, yayitha. cetā: cicetha, cicayitha. hotā: juhotha, juhavitha. tāsīty eva: yutaḥ, yuyavitha. nityam ity eva: sotā savitā, susavitha. aniṭa ity eva: lavitā, lulavitha. thala ity eva: yayiva, yayima.

pāṭhe 'tvataḥ (5.4.162)
upadeśe 'kāravatas tāsi nityāniṭaḥ parasya thala iḍ vā na bhavati. paktā: papaktha, pecitha. śaktā: śaśaktha, śekitha. pāṭha iti kim? karṣṭā: cakarṣitha. atvata iti kim? bhettā: bibheditha. taparaḥ kim? rāddhā: rarādhitha. tāsīty eva: śāntaḥ, śemitha. nityam ity eva: raddhā radhitā, rarandhitha. aniṭa ity eva: phaṇitā, pheṇitha. thala ity eva: peciva, pecima.

sṛjidṛśaḥ (5.4.163)
sṛjidṛśibhyāṃ parasya thala iḍ vā na bhavati. sasraṣṭha, sasarjitha. dadraṣṭha, dadarśitha.

ṛvṛvyeñadaḥ (5.4.164)
arter vṛñer vyeño 'tteś ca parasya thala iḍ bhavati, nityaṃ vikalpānuvṛtter vyeñada ānarthakyāt. āritha, vavaritha, saṃvivyayitha, āditha.

kvasor ekājādghasaḥ (5.4.165)
ekāca ākārāntād ghasaś ca parasya kvasor iḍ bhavati. pecivān, yayivān, jakṣivān. ekājādghasa iti kim? babhūvān. 

vā hanagamavidaviśadṛśaḥ (5.4.166)
hanādibhyaḥ parasya kvasor iḍ vā bhavati. jaghnivān, jaghanvān. jagmivān, jaganvān. vividivān, vividvān. viviśivān, viviśvān. dadṛśivān, dadṛśvān.

ṛhanaḥ sye (5.4.167)
ṛdantād dhanteś ca parasya aya ity etasya iḍ bhavati. kariṣyati, haniṣyati.

añjeḥ sicaḥ (5.4.168)
añjeḥ parasya sica iḍ āgamo bhavati. āñjīt.

stusuño 'taṅi (5.4.169)
stauteḥ sunoteś ca parasya sico 'taṅi parata iḍ bhavati. astāvīt, asāvīt. ataṅīti kim? astoṣṭa. adhāvīd iti dhuñā siddham, adhauṣīd iti dhuvā bhavitavyam.

yamaramanamātāṃ sak ca (5.4.170)
yamādīnām ākārāntānāṃ cānantarasya sica iḍ bhavati, sak caiṣām āgamaḥ. ayaṃsiṣṭām, araṃsiṣṭām, anaṃsiṣṭām; ayāsiṣṭām. ataṅīty eva: āyaṃsta pādam.

ṛsmipūṅañjaśaḥ sanaḥ (5.4.171)
ṛprabhṛtibhyaḥ parasya sana iḍ bhavati. aririṣati, sismayiṣate, pipaviṣate, añjijiṣati, aśiśiṣate.

kṝbhyaḥ pañcabhyaḥ (5.4.172)
kṝ ity evamādibhyaḥ pañcabhyaḥ parasya sana iḍ bhavati. cikariṣati, jigariṣati, didariṣate, didhariṣate, pipṛcchiṣati. pañcabhya iti kim? sisṛkṣati.

rudbhyas tiṅaḥ (5.4.173)
rudādibhyaḥ pañcabhyaḥ parasya valādes tiṅa iḍ bhavati. roditi, svapiti, prāṇiti, śvasiti, jakṣiti. tiṅa iti kim? svaptā. pañcabhya ity eva: jāgarti.

janīśīḍaḥ sdhve (5.4.174)
jana īśa īḍaś ca parasya sakārādes tiṅo dhva ity etasya ca iḍ bhavati. vyatijajñiṣe, vyatijajñidhve; vyatijajñiṣva, vyatijajñidhvam. juhotyāditvād dvirvacanam. īśiṣe, īśidhve; īśiṣva, īśidhvam. īḍiṣe, īdidhve; īḍiṣva, īḍidhvam.

āne mug ataḥ (5.4.175)
āne parato 'kārāntasya mug āgamo bhavati. pacamānaḥ, yajamānaḥ. ata iti kim? kurvāṇaḥ. taparaḥ kim? dadānaḥ. prakṛter ity eva: prāṇaḥ.

āsīnaḥ (5.4.176)
āsaḥ parasyānasya īttvaṃ nipātyate. āsīnaḥ.

pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ.


mṛjer āt (6.1.1)
mṛjer ata ād bhavati. mārṣṭi, mārṣṭā. ata ity eva: mṛṣṭaḥ.

ṛto 'ci vā (6.1.2)
mṛjer ṛkārasyājādau parata ād vā bhavati. mārjanti, mṛjanti. mārjan, mṛjan. ṛta iti kim? saṃmārjanam. acīti kim? mṛṣṭaḥ.

ajāgṛṇiśvīnāṃ sicy ataṅy ādaic (6.1.3)
ataṅpare sici parato jāgṛṇiśvivarjitāyā ajantāyāḥ prakṛter ādaico bhavanti. akārṣīt, acaiṣīt. atra pratyāsatter ikārasyaikāraḥ, ukārasyaukāraḥ, pāriśeṣyād ṛkārasyākāraḥ. śeṣāṇām asaṃbhavān na bhaviṣyati; udavoḍhām iti ḍhalopasyāsiddhatvāt. ataṅīti kim? acyoṣṭa. ajāgṛṇiśvīnām iti kim? ajāgarīt, aunayīt, aśvayīt. kathaṃ nyanuvīt, nyadhuvīd iti? antaraṅgatvād uvi kṛte vakāreṇa vyavadhānān na bhaviṣyati, halantalakṣaṇasya ca neṭi (6.1.5) iti pratiṣedhāt. alāvīd ity api tarhy okāre 'vādeśe ca kṛte na prāpnoti? nāprāpte 'deṅy ādaij ārabhyate, uvi punaḥ prāpte cāprāpte ca. na ca ṇiśvigrahaṇaṃ jñāpakaṃ sicy antaraṅgābhāvasya, ādaico 'deṅapavādatvāt. na ca prayojanam asti. yo 'py āha: acecāyīt, anenāyīt, acirāyīt, ajirāyīd iti yāntalakṣaṇaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ syāt, tatrāpi nādeṅprāptir asti, ādaicā bādhitatvāt.

halo 'caḥ (6.1.4)
ataṅpare sici parato halantāyāḥ prakṛter yo 'c tasyādaico bhavanti. apākṣīt, abhaitsīt, arautsīt, atāpsīt, arāṅkṣīt, asāṅkṣīt.

neṭi (6.1.5)
iḍādau sici parato halantāyāḥ prakṛter ādaico na bhavanti. akoṣīt.

vorṇoḥ (6.1.6)
ūrṇoter iḍādau sici parata aij vā bhavati. praurṇāvīt, praurṇavīt, praurṇuvīt.

halāder upāntasyāśvasakṣaṇahmyedito 'taḥ (6.1.7)
halāder halantasya śvasikṣaṇibhyāṃ hakāramakārayakārād editaś cānyasya yo 'kāra upāntas tasyeḍādau sicy ataṅpare parata ād vā bhavati. arāṇīt, araṇīt. halāder iti kim? mā bhavān aṭīt. upāntasyeti kim? arakṣīt. aśvasakṣaṇahmyedita iti kim? aśvasīt, akṣaṇīt; agrahīt, avamīt, avyayīt; aragīt. ata iti kim? akoṣīt. hala ity eva: avadhīt.

vadavrajalraḥ (6.1.8)
vadivrajor tāntānāṃ rephāntānāṃ ca halādīnāṃ yo 'kāras tasyeḍādau sici parata ād bhavati, nityaṃ punarvidhānāt. avādīt, avrājīt; acālīt, akṣārīt. upāntasyety eva: aśvallīt, avabhrīt.

ñṇiti (6.1.9)
ñiti ṇiti ca parata upāntasyāta ād bhavati. pākaḥ, pācakaḥ. upāntasyety eva: bhaṅgaḥ, bhañjakaḥ.

acaḥ (6.1.10)
ñiti ṇiti ca parato 'nantarasyāca ādaico bhavanti. kārakaḥ, nāyakaḥ, lāvakaḥ. babhṛveti nityatvād ake kṛte vakāreṇa vyavadhānān na bhaviṣyati.

kiti cāpatyādāv acām ādeḥ (6.1.11)
ñiti ṇiti kiti ca apatyādyarthavihite parataḥ prakṛter ye 'cas teṣām āder aca ādaico bhavanti. Dākṣiḥ, Plākṣiḥ. Aupagavaḥ. Aitikāyanaḥ. apatyādāv iti kim? kaṇḍūyati, śithilayati. acām iti kim? halāder api yathā syāt.

devikāśiṃśapādīrghasattraśreyasām āt (6.1.12)
ñṇiti kiti cāpatyādyarthavihite parataḥ prakṛter Devikādīnām acām āder aca ād bhavati. Dāvikam udakam, Dāvikākūlāḥ śālayaḥ; Pūrvadevikā nāma prācāṃ grāmaḥ, tatra bhavaḥ Pūrvaśāṃśapaḥ. Dīrghasattre bhavam, Dārghasattram. Śreyasi bhavam, Śrāyasam. apatyādāv ity eva: Devikīyati. kathaṃ Vahīnarasyāpatyam, Vaihīnariḥ? Vihīnaraśabdaḥ prakṛtyantaram asti.

kekayamitrayupralayānāṃ yāder iyaḥ (6.1.13)
Kekayādīnāṃ ñṇiti kiti ca parato 'cām āder aca ādaicaḥ siddhā eva, yakārādes tv avayavasya iyādeśo bhavati. Kaikeyaḥ, Maitreyaḥ. pralayād āgatam, prāleyaṃ himam.

aijbhāvino yvaḥ padāntāt prāg aic (6.1.14)
ñṇiti kiti cāpatyādyarthe vihite parata aijbhāvino 'caḥ sthāne yau yvau tābhyāṃ padāntābhyāṃ pūrvāv aicau bhavataḥ. vaiyākaraṇaḥ, Sauvaśvaḥ. aijbhāvina iti kim? dvyāśītikaḥ. atra hy uttarapadasyādaijvacanāt (6.1.26) pūrvapadasyādaicām abhāvaḥ. kathaṃ Pūrvatryalinde bhavaḥ, Pūrvatraiyalindaḥ? atrāpy uttarapadastho 'yam acām āder aca aijbhāvinaḥ sthāne yakāra itikṛtvā bhavaty eva. yva iti kim? dvaimāturaḥ. padāntād iti kim? Yataś chāttrāḥ, Yātāḥ.

dvārādīnām (6.1.15)
dvārādīnāṃ ñṇiti kiti ca parato yvābhyāṃ pūrvāv aicau bhavataḥ. dvāre niyukto, dauvārikaḥ - svaram adhikṛtya kṛto granthaḥ, sauvaraḥ - vyalkaśe bhavaḥ, vaiyalkaśa iti vipūrvāt pūrveṇaiva siddham - svastīty āha, sauvastikaḥ -svar bhavam, sauvam; asaṃkhyasyānārācchaśvato 'siti (5.3.140 Gaṇa) ity antyājādilopaḥ - svargagamanam āha, sauvargagamanikaḥ - Sphyakṛto 'patyam, Sphaiyakṛtaḥ - Svādumṛdor apatyam, Sauvādumṛdavaḥ - śuna idam, śauvanam; aṇi lopābhāvaḥ. śuno vikāraḥ, śauvaṃ māṃsam; añi lopa eva - śvādaṃṣṭrāyāṃ bhavaḥ, śauvādaṃṣṭro maṇiḥ; anyeṣām api (5.2.145) iti dīrghatvam - śvo bhavaḥ, śauvastikaḥ - svasyedam, sauvam - svagrāme bhavaḥ, sauvagrāmikaḥ; adhyātmāditvāṭ (3.3.29) ṭhañ - svādhyāyena jayati, sauvādhyāyikaḥ. svagrahaṇena siddhe svagrāmādipāṭhād iha na bhavati: svāpateyam.

nyagrodhasya kevalasya (6.1.16)
nyagrodhaśabdasyāsamastasya ñṇiti kiti ca parato yakārāt pūrvam aij bhavati. naiyagrodhaś camasaḥ. kevalasyeti kim? nyāgrodhamūlāḥ śālayaḥ. etac ca jñāpakaṃ tadādividheḥ, vyutpattipakṣe niyamārtham, avyutpattipakṣe vidhyartham.

na vyatihāre (6.1.17)
anyonyakriyākaraṇe yvaḥ padāntāt prāg aij na bhavati. vyāvakrośī, vyāvacarcī. striyāṃ ṇac (1.3.76), tasmād aṇ (4.4.21).

svāgatādīnām (6.1.18)
svāgatādīnāṃ ñṇiti kiti ca parato yvaḥ padāntāt prāg aij na bhavati. svāgatam ity āha, svāgatikaḥ - svadhvareṇa carati, svādhvarikaḥ - Svaṅgasyāpatyam, Svāṅgiḥ - Vyāṅgiḥ - Vyāḍiḥ - vyavahāreṇa carati, vyāvahārikaḥ.

śvāder iti (6.1.19)
śvaśabdāder ikārādau ñṇiti kiti ca parato yvaḥ prāg aij na bhavati. Śvabhastrasyāpatyam, Śvābhastriḥ. śvagaṇena carati, śvāgaṇikaḥ. kathaṃ Śvābhastrer idam, Śvābhastram iti? iñi lupte 'pi tatkṛtaḥ pratiṣedho bhavaty eva. itīti kim? śauvādaṃṣṭro maṇiḥ.

padasya vā (6.1.20)
śvaśabdādeḥ padāntasya ñṇiti kiti ca parato yvaḥ prāg aij na bhavati vā. śvāpadam, śauvāpadam.

uttarasya (6.1.21)
uttarapadasya ñṇiti kiti ca parato 'cām āder aca ādaico bhavanti. adhikāraś cāyam.

aṃśād ṛtoḥ (6.1.22)
avayavāt parasyottaravācina uttarapadasya ñṇiti kiti ca parato 'cām āder aca ādaico bhavanti. pūrvavārṣikaḥ. varṣāṇām ayaṃ pūrvabhāge pūrvaśabdaḥ. avayavo 'pi samudāyaśabdenocyata iti pūrvāś ca tā varṣāś ceti viśeṣaṇasamāsaḥ. aṃśād iti kim? ṛtvantarair vyavahitāsu pūrvavarṣāsu bhavaḥ, paurvavarṣikaḥ. sauvarṣikaḥ.

susarvārdhāj janapadasya (6.1.23)
susarvārdhebhyaḥ parasya janapadavācino ñṇiti kiti ca parato 'cām āder aca ādaico bhavanti. supāñcālakaḥ, sarvapāñcālakaḥ, ardhapāñcālakaḥ.

amadrāṇāṃ diśaḥ (6.1.24)
